mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕蔡利、<span style="mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕春钰、</span></span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕耿松、吕国妹、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕华</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吕丽珍</span>、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕梅霞、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕世瑜、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕巍</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吕相富、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吕月霞、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">拉珍（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村村妇，是扎陵湖乡河源新村南杰家族的女儿，已婚育有两个孩子，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>岁的女儿名叫塔嘎，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>岁的儿子名叫次嘉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">拉幕札部：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1944</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，内蒙古自治区赤峰市克什克腾旗人，蒙古族名<span lang="EN-US">Lhamjab A.Borjigin</span>，原南蒙古民俗学家协会会员、锡林郭勒联盟文学协会（现更名为锡林郭勒盟文学艺术界联合会）会员和内蒙古民间艺术协会会员，蒙古族知名历史学家兼维权作家，蒙古族人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。早在<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，曾因调查走访了中国文化大革命的生还者及其家人，随后以蒙古族文字撰写了一部旨在记录文化大革命的酷刑情况（主要指中共对内蒙古族人遭种族灭绝）的书籍，书名为《中国文化大革命》（蒙古语为<span lang="EN-US">Ulaan Huvisgal</span>）；因该书涉及敏感题材，故而当时所有国营的出版社都拒绝出版此书，最后只能通过地下出版商自费出版；后因此书不仅在内蒙古自治区及蒙古族人所在区域深受欢迎，而且也在蒙古国中很受欢迎，遂其再次出版发行，以满足蒙古族人的阅读和收藏需要；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，因其又将该书翻译成汉文出版，遂立遭中共内蒙古当局的秋后算账；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被内蒙古锡林浩特市警方抓捕后，又被以不确罪名指定居所监视住居；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，又被锡林浩特市检察院予以批捕，指控其因撰写《中国文化大革命》一书，被认定为主张民族分裂、破坏民族和谐的出版物，故应逮捕并将以涉嫌“分裂国家”、“破坏民族团结”罪名起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其案在内蒙古自治区锡林浩特市法院以“民族分裂”、“破坏民族团结”、“非法出版发行”等罪秘密审判，因其家属和辩护律师均未到场，其在自我辩护中表示，所著书中相关蒙古族人在文化大革命中的酷刑情况均属事实，故坚称自己无罪，因而法庭当天未予宣判，但最终被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月刑满出狱后，其又被当局以维稳重点对象无限期“监视居住”于家中；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，因中共针对全国各少数族裔开始全面实施强制性汉化教育，故而引发了内蒙古民众大规模的集会，抗议内蒙古学校停止使用蒙古语教学；此一事件立引内蒙古当局极度恐慌，遂在当地发起了镇压行动；为避免监控和受到更严厉的逼迫，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其成功逃亡蒙古；原本计划在蒙古国首都乌兰巴托安顿下来发布更多著作，熟料才逃离中国<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，即被<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名中国警察跨境抓捕，遣送回国，自此失联，至今下落不明；据悉，其在内蒙古的家人受牵连曾遭到多次骚扰、威胁施压，以令其尽快返回国内。目前被羁押地点缺详。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_18.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_18.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔（哈）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1986</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州人，伊犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">7</span>连<span lang="EN-US">28</span>号公民，哈萨克族穆斯林，清真寺伊玛目（政府指定的穆斯林领祷人），中国在押良心犯。自新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克族等少数族裔被中共新疆当局高压严控，采取集中教育培训（又称“再教育营”）以来，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年是被当局以各种罪由送“再教育营”，而后被再转拘捕、判刑最多的一年；腊吾尔孜拜·依孜巴沙尔虽为中共官方指定的伊斯兰教伊玛目（领祷人），也从未参加任何宗教极端势力，但<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，却被察布查尔县<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团派出所警突然带走，并送某“再教育营”接受洗脑式培训（实则关押）；后因强行教育培训过程中不与官方妥协、合作，遂于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月之后，被察布查尔县警方刑拘和逮捕，指控其“念经（古兰经）即违法”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年下半年（具体日期不详），其案在犁哈萨克自治州察布查尔县法院正式开庭审理受理，最终在无代理辩护律师及家人在场的情况下，被以“念古兰经”罪名秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">23</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2041</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。目前在新疆生产建设兵团第七师奎屯监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/10/23.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">郎东月：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市延庆区法轮功学员，女，是北京市延庆区延庆镇上水磨村人，又名郎冬月。一九九八年，她开始修炼法轮功。在中共邪党对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，郎东月曾多次被抓捕，五次被劳教，四次都是在北京女子劳教所遭迫害；一次被送辽宁马三家劳教所，累计被迫害达十年之久，曾遭受过数次令人发指的残暴酷刑和虐待。郎东月<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日在河北张家口市怀来县被抓捕、关押构陷至今，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月八日被开庭，因为事实不清，证据不足，庭审无法继续。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，郎东月被河北张家口市宣化区法院判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，罚款一万五千元，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/25/463392.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 0pt;">郎计云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山西省忻州市代县法轮功女学员，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。在<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日下午，她突然遭受到代县公安局抄家、抓捕，在抄家过程中只搜查到<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个真相光盘，就以此为借口把郎计云抓捕到代县洗脑班进行迫害，她一直给相关参与迫害的邪党人员讲真相，不配合邪恶的要求。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被代县公安局执行逮捕，关押在忻州市看守所迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并且罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445961.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: Roman&quot;;">来桂芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大连公安局国保支队同大连开发区公安分局属下五彩城派出所、湾里派出所、黄海路派出所、海青派出所、董家沟派出所等出动数十个警察，以拦路抓捕、抢劫、入室抢劫的方式在多个地点同时实施多起抓捕法轮功学员案。十名当时被抓捕的法轮功学员被非法批捕：周海燕、胡志琴（女，五十八岁）、来桂芳（女，四十二岁）、时宁瑶（女，三十八岁）、方芳（女，五十四岁）、林景萍（女，四十六岁）、贾秀春（女，四十一岁）、曹娥（女，五十五岁）、武丽艳（女，五十二岁）和刘淑芬（女，七十八岁）。八十一岁的郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。来桂芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">赖成妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广东省清远市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，家住广东省清远连州市连州镇鹅公潭村。此前，因宣传法轮功，赖成妹<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被拘禁十五天，<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日晚，广东省清远市连州市警察大规模抓捕法轮功学员，当地邵艳芳、赖成妹等<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位法轮功学员被抓捕。邵艳芳、赖成妹被关押到阳山县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被批捕。被构陷到英德市检察院后，邵艳芳、赖成妹被转移到英德市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，邵艳芳被英德市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；赖成妹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元。赖成妹刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html#zip5"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">赖天龙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州<span lang="EN-US">2020.11.12</span>大抓捕案受难者之一。民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，虽经常参与民主维权活动及与民主友人在一起的聚餐活动，但因其为人处事低调，故而一直鲜为人知；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，赖天龙与范文成、范一平、胡天峰等多人被广东省广州市国安局以“颠覆国家政权”为由抓捕，并被指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，又被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，知其被以涉嫌同罪名正式逮捕，；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，知范文成、赖天龙、范一平、胡天峰、韦亚妮等五人案被移送至广州市检察院审查起诉；之后，又于同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，案宗被移送至广州市中级法院，五人均被以“颠覆国家政权罪”起诉，案由涉及组党，具体事实无非聚餐闲聊时政、去云南旅游等；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其被认定为该案积极参与者，终被广州市中级法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。目前被羁押于广州市安全局看守所（广州市花都区迎宾大道<span lang="EN-US">111</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">510800</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/08/51112.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">雷焕英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川泸州市法轮功学员。罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英、苟正琼，家住泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，苟正琼在泸县兆雅镇给学生讲真相时，遭兆雅镇派出所警察抓捕。同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，又在泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇，抓捕了正在各自店铺里工作的法轮功学员邓万英、雷焕英、罗太会。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，被关押了两年的泸州市龙马潭区特兴镇<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名法轮功学员罗太会、雷焕英、邓万英，苟正琼，因为信仰法轮大法，在<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次庭审后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月上旬，被泸县法院判刑：邓万英<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，雷焕英<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罗太会<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，苟正琼<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。雷焕英刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E6%B3%B8%E5%B7%9E%E5%B8%82%E5%9B%9B%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E8%87%B3%E4%B9%9D%E5%B9%B4-430406.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">雷小利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陕西西安市辛家庙法轮功学员，女，她双眼近乎失明，日常生活需靠家人帮助。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，雷小利被莲湖区大莲花池派出所警察，以所谓的“在取款机上放小册子”为名，抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，她被关押在西安莲湖区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，雷小利被莲湖区法院开庭。庭上，维权律师为雷小利做了无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，家属接到雷小利被莲湖区法院冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千的通知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/22/2021-12-22.html#zip6"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">雷云波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，原荆州银行系统职工。因修炼法轮功被单位开除。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年在河南发真相资料被抓捕，后在武汉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。在范家台监狱被殴打，被超体力奴役。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年初，雷云波在云南被抓捕后，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月上旬，雷云波又被抓捕，至今仍被关押在荆州市沙市区看守所，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">长春法轮功学员。冷凤翎女士目前被关押在吉林省女子监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日家人去监狱会见，才得知她被判处刑期<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。冷凤翎<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被长春路园区国保、公安分局、长春和平大街派出所联合抓捕，并抄家，随后冷凤翎被刑事拘留，关押在第四看守所。现在冷凤翎被非法关押在吉林省女子监狱，构陷她的罪名是所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施”，目前在第八监区第五支队，人员编号：<span lang="EN-US">70010194</span>。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">楞珠扎巴（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">西藏歌手。楞珠扎巴于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被拘留，距离他<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月发行歌曲“黑帽子”不到两个月。在经过一年多的审前拘留之后，他于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑，被剥夺了辩护判权。楞珠扎巴最终判处<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年徒刑，理由是他在西藏那曲市比如县演唱批评政府镇压政策的歌曲。此前，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，楞珠扎巴与另一位著名的藏族歌手贡布丹增合唱一首名为《扎西央卓》的歌曲，其内容阐释境内藏人在中国政府的压制下遭受的状况和赞颂达赖喇嘛尊者，贡布丹增最终于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被判处三年半徒刑。楞珠扎巴曾被监禁在那格监狱，目前他所监禁的位置和健康状况尚未清楚。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李佰华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨著名民主人士于云峰妻子。于云峰、李佰华夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭哈尔滨市公安局香坊分局以“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留。本次夫妇一起被拘留具体事因未明。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉于云峰、李佰华夫妇均被以寻衅滋事罪名，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月（二审）被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，李佰华于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份已移送黑龙江女子监狱（集训队）服刑。于云峰目前还关押于哈尔滨香坊区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/202012285.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李保兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市武清区豆张庄镇周立营村法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>女，<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李保兰、齐文伯在发放法轮功资料时被豆张庄镇派出所警察抓捕并抄家。由于身体原因（血压高），她们被以取保候审的名义放回家中。但<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多来，公检法相关人员一直在构陷她们。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日左右，李保兰、齐文伯先后被开庭。李保兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，齐文伯被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，但在庭审判决后她们安全回家了。可在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她们被豆张庄派出所警察与法院执行庭的人，强行从家中抓捕到武清看守所关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/25/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%A4%E4%BD%8D%E8%80%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%A6%87%E5%A5%B3%E6%9D%8E%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E9%BD%90%E6%96%87%E4%BC%AF%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-452342.html"><b style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李冰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁康平法轮功学员。李冰于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点多钟，在班上，被康平公安局镇南派出所警察抓捕，晚上<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点多钟，警察搜的他家。后李冰被构陷到法院，并定于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日开庭。后李冰被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/12/460174.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/12/460174.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李本才：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，安徽省宿州市人，宿州市埇桥区三八街道宿涡路拂晓一号安置区<span lang="EN-US">14</span>栋<span lang="EN-US">203</span>室公民，强拆受害者，维权访民，中国在押维权人士。自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年以来，因其果园被当地政府侵占、房屋遭强拆，多次投诉而无果，遂被迫走上漫漫维权上访路；期间，因屡次进京信访维权、讨公道，曾多次被拘留，而其合法维权赔偿要求一直得不到合理解决；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾就果园被侵占和房屋遭强拆事宜向法院提起行政赔偿诉讼，但最终被宿州市中级法院驳回；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，曾因与其胞弟李本业以及另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名维权访民一起到安徽省宿州市信访局和宿州市法院大门口拉横幅，抗议法院就他们的信访案件枉法裁判、制造冤假错案，次日，遂<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人均遭当地派出所警方传唤，并给予行政拘留处罚；后其与其弟未被送入拘留所，在被扣押<span lang="EN-US">8</span>小时后终获释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，因又到宿州市信访局上访，要求解决其果园被侵占、房屋被强拆以及赔偿补足款长期未得解决等问题，宿州市信访局随即就将其要求申请又转给埇桥区信访局，遂其不得不再到区政府，并对接待官员说：“若区政府仍不给解决问题，就将到北京找党给解决”；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，突然被宿州市埇桥区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓走刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被宿州市埇桥区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天之后，其案被埇桥区公安局向埇桥区检察院移送起诉；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案一审在安徽省宿州市埇桥区法院开庭审理，后被以“寻衅滋事罪”速判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日；其不服，上诉；二审正在等待中；据悉，其被速判疑与“二十大”即将召开，当局需要维稳有关。目前被羁押于宿州市泗县看守所（安徽省宿州市泗县阀北路，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">234300</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/10/210.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚北京<span lang="EN-US">"</span>亮马桥<span lang="EN-US">"</span>举白纸行动，只是担保了白纸运动一个青年释放，在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日失联至今，可能也被检察院批捕。有朋友说她很善良，她在只见过因白纸抗议运动遭抓捕的林倩<span lang="EN-US">2-3</span>次的情况下，因为林倩感染新冠阳性，平谷派出所需要有人取保林倩，李超然处于同情和爱心，前往平谷派出所担保林倩出来并收留家中居住，直至林倩第二次被警方带走。<b>信息来源：<span 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李传芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省临沂市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已七旬。临沂市沂水县人，家住临沂市后罗庄区盛世馨园小区。李传芳给邻居们送法轮功真相资料，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被临沂市公安局罗庄分局盛庄派出所警察抓捕、构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬获悉：李传芳被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被劫入济南女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李聪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，吉林长春市农安县青山乡法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年生。李聪女士<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日在自家的油房被青山乡派出所警察抓捕，后被关押到农安县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李聪接到判决书，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚金两万元。李聪不服判决，上诉到长春市中级法院；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，长春市中级法院未经开庭就宣布维持原判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，李聪被劫入吉林省女子监狱继续关押迫害。入监后，每天晚上十二点睡、三点就被强制起来，坐小板凳。狱警纵容犯人虐待她，经常不给主食只给发糕、咸菜，逼强迫转化。在狱中，李聪一直遭受种种折磨：长时间罚站、饿刑、熬鹰、坐小凳、不准洗漱、围攻「洗脑」、人格侮辱等迫害外，还受到殴打，大冬天还开窗冻她，往她身上泼冷水。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李翠婷：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年出生，香港油尖旺区人，文员，香港逃犯条例修订草案（俗称“送中条例”、“逃犯条例”或“引渡条例”）反对者，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>·<span lang="EN-US">1</span>尖沙咀抗议者，香港理工大学抗议学生的声援者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，因中共当局在香港推出“逃犯条例修订草案”，遭到香港民众普遍反对，遂掀起“反送中”运动，并由香港民间人权阵线发起「没有国庆，只有国殇」游行，以期在庆祝中华人民共和国成立<span lang="EN-US">70</span>周年大会期间同步进行示威，由港岛铜锣湾游行至中环，向港府表达反对“逃犯条例修订草案”的要求，但却遭到香港警方的明确反对，并被公众集会及游行上诉委员会上诉后被驳回；不料港府官方的这一反对立场立即激怒了要求高度自治，“真普选”、“真自由”的香港民众的强烈反对，故有大批民众决定自我承担法律后果，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-11</span>月（国庆节期间及之后数十日），在港多区自行发起“反对逃犯条例修订草案”示威抗议行动；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李翠婷与约<span lang="EN-US">100</span>名示威者在声援被实弹警察围城的香港理工大学（以下简称“理大”）抗议学生时，在突破警方封锁线从校内逃走时，被女警打倒在地，并被以“参与暴力”为由野蛮拘捕；之后又被警方指控，因参与声援抗议行动时向警方“投掷汽油弹”，并与多人统一“身穿深色衣物、戴面罩及手持雨伞等”，故被以涉嫌“参与暴动罪”交由香港区域法院提堂聆讯；此间虽有暂时交保释放，但后又被收监，并与同期被捕的另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名抗议<span lang="EN-US">/</span>声援者（共<span lang="EN-US">9</span>人案）一同转交到香港西九龙裁判法院受审；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其终被该法院以“暴动罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日；另<span lang="EN-US">8</span>人亦被以“暴动罪”和“管有攻击性武器罪”分别判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年不等刑期。目前在香港罗湖惩教所（香港新界上水河上乡路<span lang="EN-US">163</span>号）服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/49.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/49.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李存国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东泰安市法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,1959</span>年生。李存国是泰安市退休职工，他妻子谢清玲是泰安市化肥厂退休职工。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其妻子谢清玲被泰山区法院视频开庭，而后被冤判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，罚款两万元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日下午，李存国被泰山区公安分局<span lang="EN-US">610</span>和国保警察跟踪抓捕，关押在泰安市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在没有任何亲友到场的情况下，李存国被泰山区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款一万五千元。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，李存国被关押到山东省监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/7/%E5%A6%BB%E5%AD%90%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%9D%8E%E5%AD%98%E5%9B%BD%E8%A2%AB%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-463890.html"><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江苏省徐州市法轮功学，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，今年<span lang="EN-US">58</span>岁，籍贯江苏省徐州市，暂住上海市黄浦区国货路。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李德标使用网络路由器向世人讲清法轮功被迫害的法轮功，被抓捕构陷。李德标被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年（刑期：<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日<span lang="EN-US">---2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日），现被关押在上海市提篮桥监狱十监区迫害。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458690.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李德宽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省蛟河市法河沿村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年六十岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>，李德宽在蛟河市长安街的出租房内被街道派出所警察绑架，并遭非法抄家，其中有三套师父法像和很多大法书籍，家中九万五千余元现金也被警察拿走。五月一日下午，李德宽被押送到蛟河市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李德宽被吉林省蛟河市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李德生：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省广州市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年生，现年二十岁，家住广州市天河区。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，李德生在广州市海珠区一家店铺用法轮功币与人兑换整钱时，遭人恶告，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在家中被海珠区华洲派出所警察抓捕、抄家，李德生被关押到海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，李德生被海珠区法院判刑宣判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/5/454541.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李德香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">甘肃金昌市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年出生，家住甘肃省金昌市。在中共对法轮功持续迫害的<span lang="EN-US">22</span>年中，累计被监禁<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日上午，李德香在家中被滨河路派出所、龙津里社区人员抓捕，被关押在金昌市金川区看守所，后得知已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚七点多被松原市国保大队抓捕抄家。家里被抄走多部手机，两本《转法轮》、《洪吟五》一本，台历一个，对联一对，一个炼功播放器。后被关押在松原市善友看守所，最近得知他已经被庭审，李东军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现被关押在四平市公主岭监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" lang="EN-US">30</span>日李冬菊被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b minor-fareast;">李方芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">沈阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生。毕业于沈阳大学外语系，原是麦当劳东北地区营运经理。李方芳<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被抓捕，她当晚被转至铁西区公安分局，次日被劫持到沈阳市第一看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，她被沈阳市经济开发区法院开庭，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西省南昌市进贤县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生。因修炼法轮功遭多次迫害关押。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，李芳兰因父亲去世，从青海西宁儿子家里回老家奔丧，在西宁火车站进站过安检时被搜包，包里带有大法的书籍和手机，西宁火车站派出所抓捕了李芳兰，借口是扰乱社会治安秩序。后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年正月初<span lang="EN-US">9</span>她被关押到江西省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/8/451659.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/8/451659.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李凤芝：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁沈阳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共镇压法轮功，李凤芝因坚持信仰遭拘留、劳教，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被皇姑区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，因被迫害的双眼无视力被保外就医。王金凤和李凤芝于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被皇姑区黄河派出所、皇姑区国保警察抓捕构陷；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，沈阳市两位善良妇女王金凤、李凤芝坚持修炼法轮大法真、善、忍，被于洪区法院判刑：王金凤<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，李凤芝<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，各罚金五千元。李凤芝刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/4/450397.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李凤英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，五莲县法轮功学员李凤英、郑允美在五莲县大郭村集讲法轮功时被警察抓捕。随后，警察去李凤英、郑允美住处抄家，抢走大法书籍、打印机、笔记本电脑、法轮功币、护身符、法轮功台历等物品。警察又抓捕了法轮功学员王世花、王洪武及流离失所的潍坊学员杨明珍。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>位法轮功学员遭警察审讯后，均被关押到日照市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日五人均被五莲县法院判刑：李凤英<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，王洪武<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，杨明珍、郑允美<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王世花被<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/22/461141.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李钢：女，</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">大连市沙河口区法轮功学员。李钢老人<span lang="EN-US">1943</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月生，两年前，老人曾被绑架，被非法批捕，但因身体亮起红灯，被非法关押在看守所<span lang="EN-US">80</span>天后，于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚回家。后于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日遭绑架、构陷，大连市沙河口区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李根山：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，汉族，宁夏动物与环境保护志愿者。户籍所在地为宁夏回族自治区中卫市沙坡头区农牧厂。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，李根山因参与举报腾格里沙漠排污案引发关注。涉事企业是他曾经供职的宁夏美利纸业集团有限公司。污染案曝光后，生态环境部挂牌督办。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他与其他志愿者一同举报了持枪盗猎案，获得<span lang="EN-US">1500</span>元人民币奖励。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，他又举报了宁夏三元中泰冶金有限公司罐车偷排废水问题。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，李根山一直在举报当地风力发电项目未经审批开工建设的问题。其认为中卫市的风力发电项目可能会破坏国家二级保护动物黄羊的栖息地。栖息地所在的麦垛山有两个风力发电项目，分别属于宁夏中卫宁清风力发电有限公司和宁夏中卫麦垛山新能源有限公司。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，宁夏回族自治区中卫市公安局沙坡头区分局抓捕了李根山。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>被以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，李根山人被以涉嫌非法猎捕、杀害珍贵野生动物罪，敲诈勒索罪，寻衅滋事罪被中卫市沙坡头区人民检察院批准逮捕。李根山被抓捕在网络上引起争议，有网友指他是因为举报环保问题而遭到了报复。但中卫警方回应称，此案与举报环保问题无关，警方是在依法办案。后于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日李根山被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李广清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北云梦县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>出生，家住云梦县邱聂大队。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日晚上，李广清在云梦县黄香大道与建设东路交汇处给路人赠送法轮功法轮功资料时，被<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个穿黑衣服的警察抓捕到云梦县城关水陆派出所，随后被刑事拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被警察入室抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，她被葫芦岛市连山区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，李桂华被关押到辽宁省第二女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李国爱</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：秦皇岛市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，秦皇岛市山海关公安分局在左洪涛、崔秋荣夫妇开的“佳合中介”抓捕了夫妻二人及吴文章、杨晓勇、袁素静及李国爱等五名法轮功学员，抄查中野蛮地抢劫了中介周转资金十余万元现金及电动车一辆和其它办公用品。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，对李国爱、吴文章、左洪涛、崔秋荣等人以莫须有的罪名批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，昌黎县法院对四名法轮功学员左洪涛、刘长富、吴文章、李国爱与左洪涛的妻子崔秋荣（不炼功）五人开庭。后判处左洪涛<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年有期徒刑，吴文章<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，李国爱<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刘长富<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，左洪涛妻子崔秋荣（没炼功）<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年零几个月（已获释）。李国爱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李国庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。在电力公司电力调度室任职调度长。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被刑事拘留、关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李国庆刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><b minor-fareast;">李国欣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省平顶山市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年生。现年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。李国欣于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日上午在平顶山河滨公园，被平顶山市湛河区南环路派出所抓捕并抄家。平顶山市公安三分局批捕，当时被关押在舞钢看守所。被关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>个多月，近悉已被鲁山县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，转到郑州监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李海艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南昆明市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年修炼法轮功。为宣传法轮功真相，李海艳利用回家乡探访亲友的机会，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日晚，在通海县城东苑小区散发法轮功真相资料，被通海县公安局抓捕，并被通海县法院以莫须有的罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；在县公安局、看守所及监狱关押期间遭到铐重镣、双手反铐、不让睡觉、强行抽血、打骂和欺凌被迫害得全身浮肿，不能站立及正常行走。唐玉、李海艳两女士<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时，在昆明市西山区卢家新村路边向路人散发法轮功宣传品，后被抓捕。当局指控两位善良女士犯了所谓“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被昆明市西山区法院视频开庭，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日下达判决书（<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>）云<span lang="EN-US">0112</span>刑初<span lang="EN-US">758</span>号，唐玉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月、罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">8000</span>元；李海艳被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元。李海艳</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李怀庆：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">重庆民营企业家。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日李怀庆忽然被重庆警方以“涉黑”的名义抓捕，同时被抓捕的还有其妻子包艳以及其儿子并公司的<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名员工（其中<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名员工均已离职）。随后，警察冻结了其公司和个人的近亿元资产。家属和律师收到的李怀庆的罪名先是“涉黑”，现在又改成“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，家属和律师原本已经收到了重庆市中级人民法院在这一天开庭审理李怀庆案件的通知，可诡异的是，家属和律师很快又收到一纸延期审理的通知书。这一延期，延到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月还音讯全无。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月在重庆开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，李怀庆被庆市第一中级法院以煽动颠覆国家政权罪、诈骗罪、敲诈勒索罪、非法拘禁罪四项罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年徒刑。李怀庆是于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被警方以涉黑名义抓捕，其名下资产同时被全部冻结。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日家属收到重庆市南川监狱的信件，告知李怀庆已转到该监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市河北区法轮功学员。李慧和郑庆兰<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日因讲法轮功真相被抓捕，李慧、郑庆兰被关押在天津河北区看守所。近一年于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点再次被河北区法院开庭。李慧被原判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月<span lang="EN-US">, </span>郑庆兰原判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/24/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E6%85%A7%E3%80%81%E9%83%91%E5%BA%86%E5%85%B0%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441653.html"><b lang="EN-US">12</span>月被重庆石桥铺高新区公安分局抓捕，被劳教两年，关押在重庆茅家山女子劳教所。。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日重庆<span lang="EN-US">5</span>名法轮功学员李嘉惠、张盛全、李玉华、高洪伟、秦雪美被抓捕，两年多后<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月才获悉已经被判刑。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">哈尔滨市道里区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，被道里分局国保警察抓捕，后李继武被道里法院判三年，<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李健：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东广州法轮功学员，女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州中山大学退休教师，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月出生，广西横县人，大学毕业，住中山大学南校园西北区。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，因去北京上访，她曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，关押到广州市槎头女子劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月在家被海珠区公安分局及新港街派出所警察抓捕、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。上诉后，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/5/451530.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/5/451530.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李建新</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：广东省惠州市人，人称“惠州区伯”，实名举报人。因长期网上实名举报广东惠州官员的贪腐行为，引起媒体关注和社会热议。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日因其举报惠州市副市长黄锦辉，随遭遇报复性砍伤并被泼硫酸，导致其一只眼睛失明、手脚被砍断，留下终身残疾。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日因其继续维权，坚持网络实名举报，被惠州市惠城区警方以涉“敲诈勒索罪”刑拘，后被惠阳区检察院以涉“敲诈勒索”和“非法占用耕地”二罪批捕，并被羁押于惠东县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日其被起诉于惠州市惠阳区法院，后其案又被因故移交到惠州市惠东县检察院审查起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日被广东省惠州市惠东县法院一审以“敲诈勒索罪”重判<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年代生人，河南太康县法轮功学员，本来是太康县回族小学教师。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月法轮功遭无端打压以后，因坚持信仰而屡遭迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午，李杰和法轮功学员李慧平、谷玉荣、李艳华等人到乡下散发法轮功资料，被太康逊母口镇派出所抓捕，分别关押，李杰被关押在太康看守所，李慧平等<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人被关押在周口市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月对李杰判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾基督教圣约家园教会传道。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日晚七点，临汾圣约家园教会<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余人在外举办亲子营活动，被近<span lang="EN-US">170</span>位警察冲击，当场控制同工李洁、韩晓栋，其他人员没收手机，全部被要求给开机密码，搜身，连夜带回临汾，并被等候在尧庙特警大队门口全临汾市所有派出所警察带走。警方在同工李洁、韩晓栋同工家搜查带走一些书籍资料。后李洁及其妻子李珊珊、韩晓栋被指定居所监视居住。李洁于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日因被控涉嫌“诈骗罪”被临汾市公安局刑事拘留，被羁押在山西省临汾市尧都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">省肇庆市端州区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年出生，广东省肇庆市封开县人，家住肇庆市端州区。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月李金兰开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，她被封开县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，在广东省女子监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被端州区公安分局警察抓捕，关押到端州区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被德庆县法院<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年</span>，罚金一万元。李金兰上诉后，肇庆市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李晶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">63</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日下午，李晶女士被长春市经开区分局与深圳街派出所警察抓捕并抢走她家的房门钥匙，警方后到出租屋抄家，抄走惠普高速打印机四台、激光打印机一台、电脑笔记本一台，真相电话十六部、大法书籍两套、大法真相资料等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日在经开区法院被庭审，庭审没有通知李晶家属。目前李晶仍被非法关押在长春第四看守所，现在身体出现腹部疼痛，流血现象。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日得知李晶被判刑十年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，李静在宣讲法轮功时被不明真相的人举报，遭清明街派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月得知，李静被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/8/461741.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/8/461741.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李军才<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省新乡市原阳县基督教牧师。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">近年来，因反对中共当局强拆十字架，拒绝把教堂内“爱神爱人”标语改成“爱国爱教”及在教堂内建国旗台，随遭河南省当局打压逼迫；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，被新乡市原阳县警方以涉嫌“妨害公务罪”刑事拘留，另有三名教会同工（即神职工作人员）亦被抓捕，随后几日，其所在中心堂十字架迅速被当地宗教局、公安局及城管等多个部门联合强拆，教堂内“爱神爱人”等标语被清除，教堂内被强行竖立起五星红旗；一个多月后，被抓三名同工均获取保候审，而其却被一直羁押不放，后被原阳县检察院正式批捕，指控其涉嫌“职务侵占、妨害公务和销毁账目”；截至<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其案件已在两度退回公安局补充侦查后，再次移送检察院，进入审查起诉阶段；据悉，其儿子称，当局对其父亲的一切指控均属莫须有罪名，旨在对其拒绝与官方合作态度进行刻意“打击报复”。在被关押长达<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个多月后，河南新乡原阳县家庭教会牧师李军才于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月被以“职务侵占”、“妨害公务”及“销毁账目”三罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。另三人均判缓刑。目前被羁押于新乡市原阳县看守所（河南省新乡市原阳县葛埠口乡丘庙村，邮政编号：<span lang="EN-US">453500</span>。）<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李俊华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。李俊华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李柯：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉籍，<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日生，汉族，大学学历，被捕前无业。李柯于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日从武汉乘火车前往西宁，途中换上藏袍，于次日前往塔尔寺，在下午<span lang="EN-US">2</span>点<span lang="EN-US">04</span>分购票进入寺院。并且在塔尔寺不同的地方展示标语和雪山狮子旗和<span lang="EN-US">FREE TIBET(</span>自由西藏<span lang="EN-US">)</span>标语，，让路过游客帮忙拍照。随后被塔尔寺驻寺警察拘留，随后于<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被正式批捕。该案于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日在西宁市中级人民法院审理，李柯被控煽动分裂国家罪，当庭没有宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李昆才：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">又名李坤才，河北省辛集市田家庄乡西刘家庄村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">72</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">720</span>中共江泽民集团开始疯狂迫害法轮大法后，他曾经骑自行车到北京说明法轮大法好，讲真相，因此遭迫害。在这二十多年中，他曾遭多次关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，李昆才在晋州市胡士庄寨村被田家庄乡派出所警察抓捕，关押在辛集市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月得知，李昆才被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被送往冀东分局第四监狱一监区服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/15/461999.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李兰敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生，是退休工人，家住天津市河东区泰安大街<span lang="EN-US">1</span>号。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日上午八点左右，她在家中被天津市河东区国保与中山门派出所警察抓捕，关押在河东区看守所。据警察称，李兰敏发放真相资料被人告了，经查看监控摄像头、追踪找到她的住处。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被当地法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被中级法院驳回上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被转监到天津市女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/14/462960.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李兰强：北</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">京房山区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。毕业于北京师范大学，曾在北京市海淀区太平路中学任数学教师。一九九七年十月，李兰强开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，李兰强被中共绑架，非法关押在看守所、洗脑班、劳教所、监狱迫害。曾经二次被劳教迫害共四年、被判刑三年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日晚，李兰强在发放法轮功资料时被人举报，遭西潞派出所警察抓捕，被关押在房山看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月遭房山区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#zip4"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/27/2021-12-27.html#zip4</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李蕾：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市宁河区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李国庆的妻子于波和女儿李蕾在开车出门的路上，突然被天津市宁河县公安局国保支队抓捕。随后，宁河区公安分局伙同芦台镇派出所警察又闯入李国庆的家，不仅强抢打印机、传真机等私人物品，还强行没收了他私人所拥有的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>辆车。随后李国庆、女儿李蕾被关押在芦台派出所；妻子于波被刑拘。李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人后来被关押在宁河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，检察院将构陷他们的案卷递交到宁河区法院刑事庭。近日获悉李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口都被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月李国庆<span lang="EN-US">1</span>家<span lang="EN-US">3</span>口，被关押、构陷<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年多，近日获悉被判刑：李国庆被枉判<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年、妻子于波<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、女儿李蕾<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。李蕾刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/4/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E6%9D%8E%E5%9B%BD%E5%BA%86%E4%B8%80%E5%AE%B6%E4%B8%89%E4%BA%BA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%83%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4-430403.html"><b mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李立鑫等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括李立鑫在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。李立鑫被判刑五年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html#22119233513-19"><b 0pt;">李力壮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年毕业于哈尔滨医科大学，。他曾是哈尔滨医科大学附属第一医院骨外科主治医生。曾因坚持信仰和平上访，遭多次关押、抄家，两次劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次判刑，经受了各种酷刑折磨，精神、肉体遭受了巨大的创痛，有<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年半是在囚禁中度过的。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年年初，哈尔滨疫情严重。<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，哈尔滨市香坊区<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员李力壮、霍晓辉、唐竹茵、李艳清、丁燕、焦其华、赵丽华，在车上打电话告诉世人大疫来临莫惊慌，诚念“法轮大法好，真善忍好”。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，大庆市让胡路区龙南公安分局在哈尔滨市香坊区抓捕了霍晓辉、李力壮、唐竹茵、丁燕、赵丽华、焦其华、李艳清等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员，以他们拨打“反宣”电话为名，逮捕、起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，大庆市让胡路区法院在侦查事实不清，证据不足等情况下，枉法对哈尔滨李力壮等<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功学员下达判决：李力壮被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/3/%E5%93%88%E5%B0%94%E6%BB%A8%E4%B8%83%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%80%E8%87%B3%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4-434311.html"><b
