text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">贵州省贵阳市法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">。</span>李林<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日被抓捕，先被行政拘留，关押在贵阳市三江拘留所，<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天后转为刑事拘留，被关押在贵阳市三江看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右，李林已被开庭，当庭被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。</b>此次是李林第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次被判刑，此前两次李林曾被判刑合计有<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b>：<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/15/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%8C%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-434850.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李玲莲</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：广东省梅州市梅城法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，家住广东梅州城区江南团结路，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被抓捕、抄家，后被关押在梅江区（芹洋）看守所。后李玲莲一审被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半、罚款三万五千元。后上诉，二审维持原判，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被劫持到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李美莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，江西省鹰潭市法轮功学员。自一九九九年七月，法轮功遭受江氏中共集团镇压以来，李美莲为坚持自己的信仰，告诉世人法轮功被迫害的真相，曾遭两次劳教（共计约三年多）、一次判刑（五年）。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，李美莲再次被抓捕，李美莲在江西省女子监狱脚筋被割断致残，丈夫离世，家中的儿子无人照看，生意兴旺的店铺无人料理关闭，父母双亲中有一个永远地离开了她。目前获悉其已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李麦英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东潍坊坊子区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁。山东潍坊坊子区教育局退休职工。她因坚持信仰，被多次劳教、关押洗脑迫害，多年被剥夺工作权利，工资也被<span lang="EN-US">610</span>截留。<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年底，李麦英被区国保劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，李麦英再次被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，李麦英因张贴大法好不干胶，被摄像头录影，遭到凤凰派出所警察抓捕。家中被查抄，后来被“取保候审”回家，坊子区国保大队已经对她起诉了，据说“案子”已经走到法院阶段。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，潍坊市坊子区法院人员，到坊子区教育局退休职工李麦英家，通知她要对她开庭。李麦英表示自己无罪，不会到庭。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，山东省潍坊市坊子区国保，强行将李麦英抓捕，把她劫持到坊子区法院开庭，判刑她<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。现在李麦英被羁押在何处还未知。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/1/450288.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李美荣<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: lang="EN-US">77</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月下旬，黄坤益、李美荣夫妇去单县黄冈镇发放法轮功小册子时被镇派出所警察抓捕。李美荣老人被送到菏泽市女子看守所关押，黄坤益老人因高血压被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被通过视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被判刑，李美荣老人<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，黄坤益老人<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李敏舫：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陕西省宝鸡市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1939</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，宝鸡消防厂退休职工，家住宝鸡市金台区宝平路。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被宝鸡市经二路派出所绑架到宝鸡市凌云宾馆洗脑班，<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日以取保候审的方式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，宝鸡市金台区检察院通知李敏舫已被转为监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被宝鸡市金台区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海维权人士。项文寅、徐玮、李平、俞忠欢、王国财、诸枝花等六人一行，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日去北京的国家信访局正常信访，因国家信访局没有按惯例给予短信回复，怀疑是被违法销号，所以又返回到国家信访局咨询，被北京是公安局月坛派出所拦截后移交上海市驻京办，先扣押身份证后押解回上海关押在长兴岛黑监狱，两天后的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，项文寅、徐玮、李平等三人以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，转送杨浦区看守所。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/blog-post_29.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">昆明市法轮功学员。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>多岁，黑龙江人。曾因修炼法轮功被判刑两年；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日下午，法轮功学员张晓华到官渡区子君路星云园小区朋友家串门，被警方抓捕，随后张晓华家被搜查。同时被抓捕的还有田云波、李萍等人。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日张晓华、李萍、田云波被五华区法院视频庭审，后被判刑：张晓华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，李萍<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月，田云波<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。李萍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E8%90%8D%E3%80%81%E7%94%B0%E4%BA%91%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441414.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/18/%E6%98%86%E6%98%8E%E5%B8%82%E5%BC%A0%E6%99%93%E5%8D%8E%E3%80%81%E6%9D%8E%E8%90%8D%E3%80%81%E7%94%B0%E4%BA%91%E6%B3%A2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-441414.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李其文：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东临清市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日左右被临清国保抓捕，被非关押于临清看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日李其文被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李谦：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，云南昆明法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，家住昆明市西山区白马干休所。因坚持修炼法轮功，李谦女士曾于<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日早上，因疑似派出所警察对她进行跟踪和监控，李谦只身来到昆明市棕树营派出所反映情况，并讲述法轮功被迫害真相，警察在送她出来的时候，李谦给了她几份法轮功真相资料，并嘱咐她退出邪党（党、团、队）组织才能保平安。结果被派出所警察抓捕抄家。关押在昆明市看守所。后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日李谦即被昆明市西山区公安分局逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被昆明市西山区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金一万元人民币。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被送到云南省第二女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李前伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男、身高<span lang="EN-US">1.76</span>米，<span lang="EN-US">33</span>岁，河南省漯河市人。其在浙江省宁波市工作，住在杭州市江干区。因帮助寻找胡新宇于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">21</span>点<span lang="EN-US">13</span>分离奇失踪。当日已报警无线索。开车<span lang="EN-US">(</span>白色日产蓝鸟<span lang="EN-US">)</span>从宁波阳明高速到下沙南收费站，路过下沙大桥时离奇失踪。母亲几度哭晕，老婆怀有几个月身孕，每天忍着孕吐奔波，几次晕倒。李前伟被强迫失踪，家属报案警方却不予立案。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/3_12.html<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李翘楚：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">1991</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年出生，女权主义者，劳工问题研究者。大学本科毕业于中国人民大学劳动人事学院，研究生毕业于英国约克大学并获公共政策硕士学位，其后于清华大学从事研究助理的工作。李翘楚长期参与、关注和研究中国大陆的劳工、女权和民间维权议题。她的研究领域涉及劳工视角的养老保险等政策问题。此外，她还积极参加各种民间自发行动，比如声援北京郊区“清理低端人口”事件中的农民工、反<span lang="EN-US">996</span>、<span lang="EN-US">MeToo</span>、武汉疫情下的性别暴力问题等。<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>公民案发生后，当局大规模搜捕参与厦门聚会的公民。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，李翘楚在她的男友许志永流亡期间被北京警方传唤<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时，她之后在网络发表《戴手铐跨新年：<span lang="EN-US">12</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;MS Gothic&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">∙</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">31</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">被传唤经过》，由此开始实名发声，声援<span lang="EN-US">12•26</span>案。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李翘楚被以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”被指定居所监视居住<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个。她根据自己被秘密关押的经历写下了《李翘楚：被连坐煽颠、指定监视居住的<span lang="EN-US">120</span>天》系列文章，详细讲述了自己被关押期间所遭受的酷刑及不人道虐待。当李翘楚了解到许志永在指监期间遭受酷刑后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日就伙食问题向临沂市公安局寄出了政府信息公开申请，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日就伙食远低于国家标准和高价买餐的问题对临沭县看守所进行了控告，就驻看守所检察官的不履行监督职责进行了投诉，并对临沂市公安局局长和临沂县看守所所长的违法行为进行控告。<span lang="EN-US"> 2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，李翘楚被山东警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”押往临沂，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李翘楚案被退回临沂市公安局补充侦查，期限一个月。而此前李翘楚家属申请的取保候审被驳回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日代理律师会见了李翘楚，翘楚狱中病情加重。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">家属申请取保候审再次被口头拒绝。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，律师第<span lang="EN-US">7</span>次视频会见李翘楚。得知李翘楚在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日和<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日两次外提到临沂市第四人民医院就诊，医生增加了治疗幻听的药物，服用后她的幻听症状有所缓解。但不系统的治疗，导致了翘楚月经闭经，虚胖等严重副作用。李翘楚母亲特别担忧翘楚的身体和精神状况，已第<span lang="EN-US">10</span>次申请取保候审，此前全部申请均被拒绝。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">目前李翘楚被关押在临沂市看守所。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">）<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，李翘楚代理律师收到临沂市人民检察院于今年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日提交至中级人民法院的起诉书。起诉书列出李翘楚数条“罪证”：与许志永系恋人关系，为许搭建个人博客，宣扬颠覆国家政权思想，并以此认定李翘楚煽动颠覆国家政权、推翻社会主义制度，其行为应以煽动颠覆国家政权罪追究其刑事责任。此前，李翘楚幻听的症状加剧，伴随意识模糊，精神恍惚，家人申请对其取保候审均遭拒绝。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_36.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/03/blog-post_36.html</span></b></a></span><b minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/7-10.html"><b minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/7-10.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李峭松：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，广东化州市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。自中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功以来，李峭松因坚持讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，多次被抓捕，在劳教所、洗脑班、监狱被关押迫害，累计达<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年多。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，李峭松在天河区棠下金棠苑小区给民众派送法轮功资料，遭监控拍摄。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，他在家中，被天河区公安分局国保和棠下派出所警察抓捕，被关押到天河区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，李峭松被天河区检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被构陷到海珠区检察院，十月份，被构陷到海珠区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年秋，李峭松被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。他提出上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被广州市中级法院维持原判。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/27/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E7%8B%B1-%E5%B9%BF%E5%B7%9E%E6%9D%8E%E5%B3%AD%E6%9D%BE%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AD%E5%B9%B4-440548.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李群：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">云南省文山州砚山县法轮功学员，女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">砚山县电信局职工，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年前修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，李群屡遭中共迫害，曾三次被判刑，累计被冤狱迫害<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。李群于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年底被文山州文山市公安局国保抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉：李群被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，现被关押中。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李琛慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，陕西省西安市人，西安市高陵区泾渭上城小区<span lang="EN-US">41</span>号楼<span lang="EN-US">1</span>单元<span lang="EN-US">3</span>层<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号公民，基督徒，陕西光义爱圣印务公司监事，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被西安市高陵区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被予以正式逮捕；自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月起，因其与丈夫常玉春所注册开办的印务公司大量印刷了与基督教信仰有关的数据及图书，随引起地方当局的高度关注与警觉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，西安市文化执法部门联合西安市国家安全部门对其公司进行了查封与鉴定，现场扣押各种宗教类书籍<span lang="EN-US">21</span>万余册，后又经陕西省新闻出版和电影质量检测中心对其中《改革宗信仰》等<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书鉴定，认定该<span lang="EN-US">24</span>种图书为“未经批准擅自印刷的出版物”的非法出版物，随于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，立刻与其丈夫被西安市高陵区警方一并抓走，后被以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”指定居所监视居住；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，又被更换罪名以涉嫌“非法经营罪”刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被西安市高陵区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其二人在无印刷许可证的情况下经营印刷业务，印刷非法出版物，扰乱市场秩序，起行为均构成非法经营罪，故而应予以逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其被西安市高陵区法院一审以“非法经营罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">25</span>万元；其不服上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，经陕西省西安市中级法院二审裁决，最终依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。目前仍被羁押于西安市未央区看守所，未来将送何监狱服刑，暂不明晰。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李仕海：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省青岛平度市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年生，住青岛平度市仁兆镇李家曲堤村。一九九八年开始修炼法轮功。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，李仕海屡遭迫害，曾两次被关精神病院，一度被摧残致精神失常。李仕海于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被抓捕，被关押到河南省洛阳看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被洛阳市瀍河回族区法院庭审；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日大年三十，李仕海的律师告诉李仕海的家人，说李仕海被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前已上诉。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份，西平县公安局、检察院、法院等十多人闯到李书鸾儿媳妇家，摆开阵势对李书鸾进行庭审，并对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万元；并于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日将李书鸾关押到西平县看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">：女士，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，黑龙江大庆市杜蒙县农民、法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，李淑春被杜蒙县公安局国保便衣警察抓捕；被关押到杜蒙县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，李淑春被大庆市让胡路法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李淑云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，北京市丰台区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被北京市永定门外派出所警察抓捕，关押在北京市东城区看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李双平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山西省临汾金灯台家庭教会同工、基督徒。山西临汾金灯堂教案受害者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，山西临汾金灯堂教会九位负责人和同工被警方抓捕，其中包括曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的王晓光牧师和他的妻子、曾为信仰坐牢<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的杨荣丽姊妹。后来一些同工被取保候审，又有一些新的人被抓捕。现在还在看守所的有<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人<span lang="EN-US">: </span>王晓光牧师及妻子杨荣丽，李双平、董勇勇、赵国爱、霍壮平、吴玲娥。这七人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被移送检察院审查起诉。据悉，批捕和移送检察院审查起诉的罪名都是涉嫌“诈骗罪”。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/01/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李顺华</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：广东省茂名市茂南区</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">83</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日早上，李顺华被几名警察跟踪并带到茂南区医院进行体检，后警察将李顺华带到茂名市茂南区法院三楼，迫使她坐在椅子上听取了一份判决：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年有期徒刑和罚款<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。后被关押在茂名市第一看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李万兵：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市滨海新区汉沽法轮功学员，原是天津滨海新区统计局干部。因坚持法轮大法信仰，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年曾遭劳教迫害<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在天津市双口劳教所遭到惨无人道的迫害和奴役。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月下旬，李万兵是在讲法轮功、使用法轮功币时遭人构陷，被汉沽街派出所警察抓捕的，一度被关押在汉沽看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，现被关押在天津滨海监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/12/446129.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李卫萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南楚雄州法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日妻子李卫萍与丈夫朱忠富因向人发法轮功资料，被楚雄国保警察抓捕、抄家。被关押在楚雄市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445959.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/8/445959.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李维萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福建福州市法轮功学员。女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日晚，李亚萍、李维萍姐妹在某小区发放法轮功资料，被一私家住宅的摄像头拍到，遭这家人举报。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，福州晋安区岳峰派出所抓捕了李亚萍、李维萍姐妹。后因看守所疫情期间不收人，两人被勒索人民币四千元，取保候审回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，岳峰派出所再次抓捕了李维萍。姐姐李亚萍当时外出，得知消息后被迫流离失所。李维萍现被关押在闽清县拘留所，拘留十四天后，又被转到福州市第二看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被批捕。李维萍被关押近两年后，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日遭马尾区法院庭审。后得知，马尾区法院对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">.</span>刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;"> </span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/3/448465.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/3/448465.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李文波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">昆明法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年出生，，昆明市晋宁县昆阳街道办事处古城村人。中共迫害法轮功的二十多年中，李文波因为坚持信仰法轮功，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年入冤狱<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，因所在的月山小区居委会展出污蔑法轮大法及其创始人的展板，李文波致信给晋宁区公、检、法工作人员、月山小区工作人员，澄清事实，并要求撤销展板。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，古城二组因他修炼法轮功，而被村委会扣发一万块钱。李文波针对此事，写信给村委会领导，指出此种做法不合理，要求退还扣发的钱。李文波依法将两封信递交给负责的相关部门及人员，希望所反映的问题得到解决。这本是作为一个公民的合法信访行为，但却于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，接到昆阳派出所打来的电话，叫他第二天去派出所核对一个案子。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日当晚李文波被拘捕，被扣押到昆明市晋宁县看守所。这次李文波在看守所被关押<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个多月后，又因消化道出血、空腔脏器穿孔、肠梗阻、重度贫血等严重疾病，不适合继续关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李文波以取保候审形式回家。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，西山区法院对“取保候审”在外的李文波开庭审理，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月上旬，李文波接到了昆明市西山区法院对他判刑五年，并处罚金一万元，还要销毁从他家中搜走的私人书籍及材料。李文波当即表示要上诉。未收监。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午，李文波在公共汽车站炼功，被人恶意举报后遭警察抓捕抄家。后李文波被关押在晋宁县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，昆明市西山区法院又对李文波开庭。之后，李文波家属接到了西山区法院的判决，李文波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年（加上之前正在上诉被判的五年）。李文波不服判决，向昆明市中级法院上诉，但中院依然维持了原判。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李文波被关押到云南省第一监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李文明</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年出生，甘肃省兰州市人，原名李明义、李明一，原甘肃省兰州机车厂职工，法轮功信仰者，原兰州市七里河区法轮功辅导站负责人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，曾因信仰和负责兰州七里河地区法轮功信仰者的管理工作，被当地警方从工作单位非法抓捕，至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月后才被释放；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年，曾因前往北京上访，被北京警方非法关押<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，曾因参加被迫害致死的兰州法轮功信仰者姚宝荣的悼念，被警方当场抓捕，后被送至兰州市平安台劳教所劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月—<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因在获释后又被当局强迫接受洗脑教育，其不堪受辱虐待而逃离洗脑班，遂被警方悬赏通缉；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被兰州市七里河区警方再次拘捕，并被关押于兰州市第一看守所；后其案被当地城关区检察院起诉，并被很快移交至兰州市城关区法院；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被该法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，后送甘肃省兰州监狱服刑；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，刑满出狱；据悉，狱中其遭严重迫害，多次受恶徒殴打，遭坐“老虎凳”、电击和关禁闭室等酷刑折磨，同时因自幼是孤儿，其妻肖彦红亦因信法轮功而被判刑，故长期以来无人探监；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，因常在街上与人宣传法轮功，又与另<span lang="EN-US">7</span>名法轮功信仰者被兰州市七里河区警方以涉嫌邪教罪从住处抓走刑拘，后另<span lang="EN-US">7</span>人五天后被取保获释，而其仍被续押；现其已被七里河区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，并其案应被检察院提起公诉。目前被羁押于兰州市七里河西果园看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底，他被兰州市城关区检察院起诉到城关区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月得知，城关区法院已对李文明开庭，判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金三万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/20.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/20.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/9/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E9%87%8D%E5%88%91%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E6%9D%8E%E6%96%87%E6%98%8E%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-463993.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省洛阳市洛龙区法轮功学员，女。原家住洛阳市老城区，她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月因给人讲法轮功真相遭警察抓捕；于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被老城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。洛龙区公安局警察在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底分别抓捕了刘桂花、李晓燕等法轮功学员，把她们关押在洛阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省洛阳市洛龙区法院对法轮功学员刘桂花、李晓燕做出判刑，判刘桂花<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，李晓燕<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。李晓燕刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/17/450852.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/17/450852.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李贤芝</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：湖北省襄阳市樊城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，女，湖北省襄阳市粮局退休职工，家住湖北襄阳樊城区。李贤芝于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月开始修炼法轮功。中共江泽民团伙<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月发动迫害法轮功的运动后，李贤芝遭到中共人员的抓捕、关押、骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，李贤芝因讲法轮功再次被警察抓捕，法院企图对她收监——因为前段时间（日期待查）她被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，后因被警察抄到法轮功资料，又被加刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。她因体检不合格被看守所拒收。之后法院多次要求她到医院体检。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李贤芝被警察抓捕到第一看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底，她被关押到湖北省女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/7/461708.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/7/461708.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南省辉县市人，辉县市城关镇吕巷村居民，南都网深圳法制频道前记者和编辑，疫苗受害者家长，维权公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。李新是“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人何方美的丈夫。李新为人性格温和，从不和人起冲突；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因追求自由理念而逃离中国大陆，并于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日持短期旅游签证经香港抵达印度申请政治庇护，但因其签证很快到期，而未能及时获取庇护，遂辗转到泰国准备向美国官方提出庇护申请；然当其到达泰国后，被中方知晓，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被中国警方跨境抓捕回国；获释后，因其当时<span lang="EN-US">1</span>岁<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月龄的幼女打了政府指定的百白破疫苗之后导致全身瘫痪，其多方求助均遭拒绝，遂与妻子何方美（“疫苗宝宝之家”维权团体发起人）一起投诉维权，要求当局关注并给予合理赔偿和救治；然地方当局却一拖再拖，其夫妻二人被迫进京上访，故又频遭报复与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，因其在北京逗留且为疫苗致瘫女儿上访，与此同时，其妻何方美因在辉县市政府门前怒而泼墨被警方扣押，故而其被辉县各级维稳部门多次电话强逼离开北京，并以停其手机号码相威胁；为此，其向原籍村委会提出<span lang="EN-US">4</span>点要求：“<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、回去后能见到妻子十三妹和孩子们，让十三妹自由；<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、女儿能够顺利看病治疗；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、兑现以前承诺的国家赔偿；<span lang="EN-US">4</span>、撤去监控，以后不再跟踪监控他们一家”；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李新被辉县市维稳人员通过微信定位找到后随即带走，走之前仅在微信上留言一句：“我被他们带走了”，自此长期失联；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其妻何方美被辉县市警方以涉嫌“重婚罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”正式逮捕，此时，才有消息传出，河南省辉县市政府（含维稳办人员、辉县警方、辉县市检察院及法院等）为报复其夫妇二人的上访维权，刻意伪造假证，构陷其二人涉嫌“重婚、寻衅滋事”二罪；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月左右，其在家属不知情的情况下，被辉县市法院以“重婚罪”和“寻衅滋事罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。目前在河南省焦作市监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/5_17.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/5_17.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李新德：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，从<span lang="EN-US">80</span>年代从事业余新闻报道工作，到<span lang="EN-US">90</span>年代末从事专业新闻报道工作。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日创办中国舆论监督网，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发布《下跪的副市长——山东济宁市副市长李信丑行录》，<span lang="EN-US">46</span>天后，李信被逮捕，最终被判无期徒刑。李新德成为新闻界的新闻人物，被誉为中国民间舆论监督第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>人。李新德利用网络反腐维权的事迹，许多媒体均与报道。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，江苏省邳州市公安局以李新德涉嫌“经营罪”指定居所监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月后的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日转为刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日经邳州市检察院批准逮捕。现羁押在邳州市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，江苏省邳州市法院以“经营罪”判处“中国舆论监督网”创办人李新德有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李新德刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李新兰</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：河北省张家口市万全区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年前，李新兰在北京二女儿家<span lang="EN-US">(</span>照看孩子<span lang="EN-US">)</span>期间，因向世人传递真相，曾被北京公安抓捕，后被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，李新兰在河北省张家口市宣化区大女儿家居住时，被北京公安与宣化公安联合抓捕，后被北京公安带回并判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%89%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-439997.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李行军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员，荆州市实验中学的老师。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多钟，李行军从母亲家出来，刚下楼，就被国保、西门派出所警察、学校保卫科等多人抓捕，他们对他拳打脚踢，打的满脸是血。被强行带上警车后，就送到西门看守所去了。妻子孙江怡也被抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日才开庭。李行军、孙江怡夫妇被庭审，两人都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李秀莲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东珠海市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十九多岁，家住广东省珠海市香洲区，一九九九年一月份开始修炼法轮功。中共迫害法轮功后，李秀莲多次抓捕、劳教。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日被抓捕。后李秀莲已被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/14/449589.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/14/449589.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省伊春市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生，家住黑龙江省伊春市金林区，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份开始修炼轮功，后因修炼法轮功李秀云遭到当地中共人员的骚扰、抓捕、抄家、强行洗脑、拘留等迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，伊春市金林区奋斗派出所的警察闯入李秀云的家中抄家，并抓捕了李秀云和她的丈夫，后将她未修炼的丈夫放回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被金林区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，距她被抓捕仅四个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453263.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453263.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">李雪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">山东胶州法轮功学员。一家人因信仰被迫害多年。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，李雪及其母亲宋桂香通过快递分别向北京最高检察院、最高法院邮寄了刑事控告书，控告江泽民发起对法轮功学员的迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，以阜安派出所负责人想找她们母女“谈话”的名义将宋桂香、李雪骗至派出所，然后羁押于青岛普东看守所进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李雪被判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年重刑，现在山东省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李学志；</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，重庆市渝北区龙兴镇人。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年因为耕地被强占，房屋被暴力强拆，开始维权。曾与被强征强拆的以及其他人权受害者共同维权，参与重庆地区维权活动。李学志于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点被重庆市公安局渝北区分局多名警察带走，<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留，目前在渝北区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_94.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_94.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李亚萍：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">福州法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生。原在江西省鹰潭铁路车辆段工作，退休后随夫居住在福州。李亚萍于一九九七年开始修炼法轮功。在中共对法轮功持续二十多年的迫害中，李亚萍曾被劳教两年，<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，除此之外还多次被拘留，流离失所，历尽艰辛。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，李亚萍在福州市永泰县葛岭镇散发法轮功资料时，被当地派出所警察抓捕，后李亚萍被关押在福州第二看守所，近一年后又遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/26/%E7%A6%8F%E5%B7%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BC%AA%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%B8%E5%93%A1%E6%9D%8E%E4%BA%9E%E8%90%8D%E5%86%8D%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464581.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://big5.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/26/%E7%A6%8F%E5%B7%9E%E6%B3%95%E8%BC%AA%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%B8%E5%93%A1%E6%9D%8E%E4%BA%9E%E8%90%8D%E5%86%8D%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-464581.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李彦春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1951</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河北省秦皇岛市人，原多家医院管理工作者、院长，医学专家，学科带头人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。曾从事医学专业<span lang="EN-US">40</span>多年，拥有丰富的医院管理经验；退休前，曾在当地多家医院从事管理工作并担任过院长；曾发表过<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余篇医学科技论文并担任本学科带头人；然而，虽其（含其妻子裴玉贤）职业生涯及其敬业、努力给社会与民众带来了可喜的贡献，但却因信仰法轮功而遭致中共当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，因其夫妇二人到秦皇岛市卢龙县散发法轮功宣传挂历，被恶人告发，随被卢龙县双望派出所警方抓捕，且被戴手铐、脚镣等，审讯时，惨遭殴打和刑讯逼供；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其夫妇二人涉邪教案被卢龙县警方递交到卢龙县检察院，后被卢龙县检察院以涉嫌邪教罪予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其案在秦皇岛市昌黎县法院开庭受理；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被河北省秦皇岛市昌黎县法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，后因身体极差原因被准予保外就医；其妻裴玉贤亦被以同罪名判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；二人不服判决，当庭均表示上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其被秦皇岛市卢龙县双望派出所警方再次收监逮捕，旋即被送往监狱接续服刑；其妻裴玉贤亦在此前被送河北省石家庄女子监狱服刑。目前在河北省冀东监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/76.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李艳杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，李艳杰被大庆市局伙同让胡路岗龙分局警察抓捕并抄家，说是李艳杰在让胡路明湖花园小区发放法轮功资料。李艳杰自<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日被抓捕后一直被关押在大庆市第二看守所，家人探视权被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，家人委托律师到看守所看望李艳杰，才知道李艳杰被大庆市让葫路区法院秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李艳秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁锦州市太和区，法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十二岁。她修炼法轮功十多年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李艳秋在向世人发送法轮功台历时，遭锦州太和区国保大队警察绑架，李艳秋家中的电脑、大法书籍等私人物品，被警察强行拿走。后她被关押到锦州市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日上午，锦州市太和区法院在不通知家属的情况下，在锦州看守所对李艳秋秘密开庭，法院指定了法律援助律师为她作有罪辩护，而李艳秋一直没有认过罪。法官在李艳秋身体极度虚弱、不能独立行走、不能完整表达意愿的情况下，匆匆走了过场。后获知李艳秋已经被重判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李延贺（笔名富察）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">台湾出版人，“读书共和国八旗文化”总编辑。出生于中国辽宁省，曾任上海文艺出版社副社长。其<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年移居台湾，在台湾创立八旗文化，其出版社出版了不少西方人撰写与中国相关的书籍，这些书在意识形态上算是中国大陆的禁书。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月其回大陆探亲时，在上海被中共有关部门抓捕，予以“监视居住”，李延贺彻底失去人身自由，家属和律师都无法见到本人，音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_23.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/blog-post_23.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李延香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日出生，山东省平度市人，平度市古岘镇山头村居民，青岛市即墨市大信镇“福顺废旧物品回收站”经营者，维权访民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，因其夫妻在青岛市即墨市大信镇开办一家“福顺废旧物品回收站”，生意兴隆，遂被当地大信镇派出所民警孙典东要求收中小企业保护费，一次打底<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元；因其夫妇二人对此拒绝并进行了举报，遂遭地方当局的打击报复；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，即墨市大信镇政府在无任何手续的情况下，以违法占压麦田为由将其废品回收站进行了强拆，致使其价值<span lang="EN-US">50</span>余万元私人财产掩埋损毁，数万元贵重物品在失去防护设施后被盗窃；其被迫维权讨说法，但几年来因政府机制腐败，不仅毫无果效，而且于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月在青岛市中级法院开完庭后返家途中，被法官打电话以“谈话”名义诱骗回去竟被司法拘留了<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日；后因其坚持逐级上访不停歇，故遭地方当局官官相护的肆意打压和报复，曾多次被非法拘禁、训诫、恐吓和刑拘；自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年以来，因在北京上访，曾先后被警方以“非正常上访”、“扰乱乱公共场所秩序”为由行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次，被训诫<span lang="EN-US">8</span>次；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，因再次到北京市天安门“非正常上访”，而被北京市西城区府右街派出所警方抓走，次日被遣返原籍，而后被山东省平度市警方处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被平度市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”转为刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被平度市检察院以同罪名转正式批捕，指控其罪责有三：一是<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月在黑龙江庆安火车站举牌声援被警方击毙的徐纯合，二是在山东潍坊公园和多人拉横幅示威，三是曾两次到北京天安门和中南海周边上访；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其案在青岛市第二看守所第九审判庭开庭审理，至<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其被山东平度市法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，上诉；后经二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，刑满释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉，其在出狱后因其夫妇二人继续维权抗争，二人都被平度市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘、逮捕。目前其被羁押于青岛市第二看守所，其丈夫李洪财被羁押于青岛市过渡性看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_85.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李燕玲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川广安市广安区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span
