mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李燕群：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，广东省佛山市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，李燕群曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在广东省女子监狱被虐待迫害的身体不能自理，手脚都严重变形了，至今还未完全康复。因行动不便，老人很少出门。李燕群女士一个人居住，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，在家中被中共抓捕和抄家，一直被非法关押在佛山市第三人民医院（精神病医院）。当局以防疫为由，拒绝家属和辩护律师会见。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，李燕群被佛山市禅城区法院视频庭审。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，律师被告知李燕群被判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，勒索罚金七千元，目前，家人仍然不知李燕群被非法关押在哪里。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李艺：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">上海白纸运动抗议者。艺因围观上海白纸抗议活动而被抓捕，并于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被上海警方以寻衅滋事罪名刑事拘留，现羁押于上海市徐汇区看守所。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_48.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_48.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李银欢：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省广州市越秀区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">59</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，李银欢被广州市公安局、长兴派出所警察从家中抓捕，被关押在天河区看守所。李银欢被关押和构陷一年多，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午，被海珠区法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，李银欢被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，罚金六千元。从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月开始，广州社保停发了她的养老金。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/29/462468.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/29/462468.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李银秀：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人梁子亮的妻子，梁子亮和李银秀<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李玉春：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">鞍山法轮功学员。</span>李玉春于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日在铁西区八家子附近向路人讲法轮功时，被人举报，被八家子派出所抓捕、抄家、构陷。后李玉春被冤判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/13/457709.html#2331223130-32"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/13/457709.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉娥：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省沈阳市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，准备乘火车去外地看望生病的父亲，在沈阳火车站安检时，被查出携带有法轮功的物品，后被沈阳火车站派出所警察孙斌等人抓捕，搜出大法书<span lang="EN-US">1</span>本，法轮功真相粘贴、真相币、护身符、播放器等。随后，她被关押到沈阳市看守所数月。在没有通知家属的情况下，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，李玉娥被沈阳市于洪区法院远程开庭，一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。李玉娥不服一审判决，随上诉至沈阳市中级法院。中级法院二审于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月开庭，刑期改判为<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李玉荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省九江市人，九江市濂溪区公民，微信公众号“仁即博爱”持有者，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。因常在其微信公众号“仁即博爱”发时政性贴文及视频讯息，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，遂被江西省九江市浔阳区国保警方跨区带走；带走时，先说是口头传唤，但之后即转为以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其女儿在微信朋友圈发出“告亲友书”，通报其父李玉荣已于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被浔阳区公安局国保跨区抓捕刑拘，但尚未收到拘留通知书，并表示全家人以及其他亲属都十分担心，不知其是否安康；随后，有网友查询其公众号，发现其公众号“仁即博爱”的文章已经被删除，故其本次被抓原因应与中共二十大召开，其网络言论令当局不安有关；后获悉其因言获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。目前被羁押于九江市看守所（江西省九江市庐山区八里村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">332000</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/1.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/1.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李昱函：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">岁，现北京执业律师，<span lang="EN-US">709</span>王宇案的代理律师。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年考取律师资格，<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年开始在辽宁执业。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年为逃避公安迫害从辽宁逃到北京，目前于北京市敦信律师事务个人所执业。李昱函患有心脏疾病，并曾多次受到公安的酷刑对待。李昱函律师最后一次和外界接触是在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。当天，她向弟弟发短信，说自己被沈阳市公安局和平分局警察带走。之后便下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日下午，李昱函的家属对外透露，李律师现已被沈阳市公安局和平分局以涉嫌寻衅滋事罪刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被正式批捕。律师已获会见。获知李昱函患有房颤心律失常、冠心病、甲亢、弥漫性胃炎等病，她包里的诊断证明都有，抓捕他在派出所里，她就感觉这次就活不成了。此案被当局故意拖延了近<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年的时间，不审不判。目前李昱函羁押在沈阳市第一看守所。沈阳市和平区法院定于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日开庭审理，但开庭当日却取消了开庭。根据该法院报请最高人民法院人民法院批准，本案一次次延期。案件最近一次再次被延期到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。李昱函会见律师说：“法官让我认罪认罚，我说我没有罪，怎么认呢？法官说检察院的量刑建议是<span lang="EN-US">5</span>～<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。”<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李玉新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京市海淀区法轮功学员，住</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京市海淀区苏家坨柳林村<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，李玉新送给一个不明真相的人一本法轮功册子，被其人恶意举报，当天被抓捕到海淀区看守所。据悉，在<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月中旬，李玉新被海淀区山后法院判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源： </b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/14/457739.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/14/457739.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李源东：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省茂名市法轮功学员、广东化州人，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月出生，大学毕业后进入广东省茂名港务监督局工作。李源东<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月开始修炼法轮功，但两个月后，中共开始了对法轮功的疯狂镇压，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年给信访局写信、并<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次去北京为法轮功上访，茂名市公安局因此两次对李源东劳教各<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，遭酷刑虐待，妻离子散。为求生计，到广州打工，又给民众讲述法轮功被迫害的真相，结果被恶意举报。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2019</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日</span>被广州市海珠区公安分局沙园派出所警察刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日被海珠区检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被构陷到海珠区检察院，<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被构陷到海珠区法院。关押在广州市海珠区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，李源东被海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。李源东当庭表示要上诉。在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月份已被转去韶关北江监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/9/2/%E5%8E%9F%E8%8C%82%E5%90%8D%E6%B8%AF%E7%9B%91%E5%B1%80%E5%85%AC%E5%8A%A1%E5%91%98%E6%9D%8E%E6%BA%90%E4%B8%9C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%85%AB%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-430337.html"><b
