style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李展：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">深圳佳士案维权工人。“<span lang="EN-US">7.27</span>大抓捕”第<span lang="EN-US">37</span>天后，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初，余浚聪、米久平、刘鹏华、李展四人被正式逮捕。被抓捕已经两年，仍未开庭判决。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李占金</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：女，<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年生。北京大学退休高级工程师、法轮功学员。一九九六年开始修炼法轮功，一九九九年七月中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，李占金多次遭中共迫害，被非法拘留、强制“洗脑”，被非法劳教、非法判刑。李占金于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日上午被北京市海淀区公安分局、燕园派出所张艳辉等七个警察闯入家中抓捕、抄家。后李占金老人一直被非法关押在海淀区看守所。被绑架关押构陷近两年，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被海淀法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李志芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省兴城市法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月生，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，曾被葫芦岛市政府劳动教养<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，李志芬被兴城市公安局刑事拘留，同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月三十日被“取保候审”。兴城检察院曾于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日向法院起诉李志芬。后，李志芬流离失所多年，被定为所谓的“网逃”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，李志芬在家中再被古城派出所警察抓捕，被送到了温泉派出所，由温泉派出所警察直接送到葫芦岛看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，李志芬被兴城法院判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/3/450363.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李志宏：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1995</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，英语名：<span lang="EN-US">Li Chi-wang</span>，原英属香港籍人，现香港籍人，前香港沙田区议会主席、前沙田区议会禾輋邨选区议员，香港民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。近年来，一直在民主派“公民议政平台”上做筹委（之一），曾因多次公开发表反政府言论和多次参与反香港国安法等活动，而被中共香港当局视为违法常客，进而屡遭打压，数度被捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因在香港区议会选举中，以独立民主派身分参选禾輋邨选区，而被港警于同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日以涉嫌“非法集结”罪由被抓，后又很快保释释放，其继续参与竞选活动；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，终在“民主动力”的支持下成功胜选区议员，任期由<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起生效，直至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被香港政府硬性终止；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，因有网民发起“反国歌法、国安法大游行”，其等多人参与其中，故而又被当局拘捕，并被指控其在湾仔鹅颈桥底做出喧哗和扰乱秩序行为，导致民众起哄，因而被捕；后又因其拒保候查，遂暂获释放，但同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，又被拘捕，而后又得释放；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，因沙田区议会召开大会重选主席，遂其在没有竞争下自动当选为区议会主席，任期由<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日生效，直至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被香港政府硬性裁定其宣誓无效，实时离任沙田区议员暨主席一职；之后，其再次因“反国歌法、国安法大游行”之事被港警拘捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其扰乱秩序案在香港东区裁判法院庭审，因法官称其“虽无实质性暴力行为，但用言语辱骂警察、煽动现场其他示威者”，故裁定其“在公众地方做出喧哗或扰乱秩序行为罪”成立，并将于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日宣布判决。目前被羁押地点不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_43.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/07/blog-post_43.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李志君：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北法轮功学员，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月生，家住河北衡水市冀州区，是河北衡水市冀州区职教中心的教师。一九九五年，李志君开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日凌晨五点多，冀州警察翻墙入李志君家中，抓捕了正在睡觉的李志君，被关押在衡水看守所，狱中遭酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月获悉，被关押一年九个月后<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">李志君</span>被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/19/463152.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/19/463152.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李祝全：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林长春法轮功学员。李祝全于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年大年初一被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月转长春公主岭监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/6/18/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%AD%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E5%85%AB%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-445099.html</span></u></b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">李卓人：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Lee Cheuk-yan</span>，祖籍广东潮阳人，生于上海，长于香港，香港九龙美孚公民，基督徒，前香港职工会联盟秘书长，前英属香港香港立法局议员，前香港立法会议员，前东华三院顾问局成员，前香港大学校董会成员，前工党主席，原香港市民支持爱国民主运动联合会（简称支联会或港支联）主席，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年，曾为逃避中共“批斗黑五类”，被父母抱着举家逃往香港，后就读于香港民生书院小学及中学，并在香港大学攻读土木工程系专业；<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年大学毕业后，曾加入联合医院旗下的观塘职业健康中心，从事职业健康安全信息的宣传工作；<span lang="EN-US">1980</span>年，曾因转投基督教工业委员会，而开始处理劳资纠纷和策划大型工潮等；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年，曾参与成立职工盟，并于<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年补选中首次当选立法会议员，半年后，又在最后一届立法会改选时成功获取议席；<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2012</span>年，曾多次参选立法会新界西选区直选，并数次获取连任；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2006</span>年，因在民生立场上照顾基层及劳工权益，在政治上支持民主体制发展，反对《香港基本法》第<span lang="EN-US">23</span>条的立法等，而曾被立法会议员香港天主教监察组连续三届评为“表现满意议员”；<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年，因积极介入扎铁工人工潮，协助工人争取合理待遇，而曾使劳资共识最终成功达成，使资方答应以后每年都要就保障职工的薪酬问题与工会集体谈判；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年，曾出席维多伊利亚广场（简称维园）的六四纪念烛光晚会；<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年，在民主先驱司徒华病逝后，曾接任支联会主席，并与张超雄、何秀兰及张国柱等民主派人物成立工党，出任创党主席；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因参与多个团体及政党举行集会，抗议特首选举仅为小圈子选举，要求香港实行真普选，而遭到警方喷胡椒喷雾，又因两次提出引用《立法会（权力及特权）条例》调查梁振英在特首选举期间，被曝曾在行政会议上要求用防暴队对付示威者，及其大宅出现违规建筑丑闻等议案，而遭建制派全力反对，致使两次议案均被否决；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，香港立法会选举，其以工党名义奋力参选，终获连任新界西直选立法会议员；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日至<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，因积极参与介入香港葵青货柜码头工潮，协助工人争取合理待遇，而曾遭到和记黄埔港口集团及不少富商攻击与批评；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因表示“若香港市民接受政府推出的假普选，将来更无可能争取真普选”，同时表示“不认同政府经常强调提委会会重视民意之说法”，因提委会是小圈子选出，希望市民不要受骗，接受被操控及有筛选的选举，同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月因又出席平反六四大游行，随遭中共主导下的香港当局强烈不满与伺机打压。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2016</span>年，曾因子次介入建筑等行业工人为谋求生计而引发的罢工潮，以及不同民间联盟为争取生存权利而举行的抗议游行等，而促使罢工潮与游行抗议行动取得不同程度的良好效果；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，香港立法会选举，因在新界西地区再次代表工党参选时而败选，自此结束<span lang="EN-US">21</span>年议会生涯；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，作为支联会秘书，曾针对六四事件<span lang="EN-US">29</span>周年纪念，呼吁年轻人能“不论身份，一起反击，对抗内地威权”，并说如果维园六四烛光晚会缺少大学生，将削弱团结和展示要求的力量；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因参与未经香港警方批准的“十万基督徒为香港罪人祈祷大游行”，而被长沙湾警署带走调查，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又与多名同属前任及现任立法会议员和多名泛民主派人士共<span lang="EN-US">15</span>人，被警方统一以参与“<span lang="EN-US">2019.8.18</span>维园流水集会”为由拘捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">10</span>数人案在香港西九龙裁判法院分三案处理，期间，其等被准予各以<span lang="EN-US">1,000</span>元暂时取保候审，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月其又被收监逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，其等<span lang="EN-US">9</span>名民主派人士被西九龙法院以“参与和组织未经批准集结”罪名分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，其中，其被获刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，但因还与香港传媒大亨黎智英共同涉及<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日的另一次集会，遂追加刑期，最终被法院以“组织未经批准集结罪”、“煽惑他人参与未经批准集结罪”等多项罪名宣判，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。目前疑似在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_9.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_9.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">李宗泽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，李宗泽等<span lang="EN-US">13</span>名法轮功修炼者被北京警方抓捕，包括李宗泽在内的<span lang="EN-US">11</span>位被指控“破坏法律实施罪”。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>人被逮捕起诉涉及在疫情期间发布一些国内疫情照片及与其法轮功修炼者的身份有关。李宗泽被判刑五年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/20/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-437033.html</span></u></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">李伊棕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省济南法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。家住济南市章丘区普集镇麻秸村，他在邻近的滨州市邹平区临池镇一家耐火砖厂打工。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日下午，李伊棕打工下班后，在临池镇发法轮功材料，被临池派出所警察通过摄像监控发现。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日清晨，李伊棕正在耐火砖厂干活时，遭到临池派出所警察抓捕，随后，李伊棕被关押在邹平区看守所至今。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被山东滨州市邹平区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初，家人才得知此消息。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">栗静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，辽宁朝阳市凌源市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，朝阳市公安局，政法委，<span lang="EN-US">610</span>秘密开会策划迫害，预谋在<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日之前，要抓一批法轮功学员，向中共百年大庆“献礼”；并成立专项行动小组，电话监控，跟踪监视。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日早晨，朝阳市出动大批警力在同一时间对朝阳市法轮功学员及家属实施抓捕、抄家抢劫。据不完全统计，至少有<span lang="EN-US">27</span>名法轮功学员及家属被抓捕。凌源市公安局及派出所动用了大约<span lang="EN-US">50</span>名警察，抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">12</span>名凌源市法轮功学员。栗静是其中之一，栗静被关押在朝阳市女子看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被凌源市法院远程视频开庭。后得知：栗静被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/4/442063.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">栗新田</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：山东青岛法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日出生。山东省青岛市市北区冠县路<span lang="EN-US">109</span>号。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日被警方抓捕，被诬判刑期<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现被关押在上海市提篮桥监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/4/447238.html#228323287-23"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/4/447238.html#228323287-23</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎金凤<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省云浮市法轮功学员。黎金凤于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被云安区法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月份上诉维持原判，将在广州女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/10/13/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%B8%80%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%81%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%89%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-432491.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎容好：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省中山市小榄镇维权人士。黎容好是因为一家九口人，被地方官员以其婆婆是再婚女为由，剥夺了集体经济组织成员身份，成为了中国特色的“空挂户”，失去了生产与生存（承包地、生产劳动，股份分配，宅基地）等权利。在黎容好上访维权中，一直默默地帮助那些比自己更艰难的访民，在北京有访民形象大使之美誉，也无数次遭到包括被构陷判刑等残酷迫害。在中共十九届六中全会前夕，广东当局雇佣地痞流氓，每天<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时对黎容好实施跟踪、盯梢等维稳。为了常年上访维权的黎容好老了有个基本保障，黎容好的兄弟姐妹凑钱为其购买了社会保险，不料在冤案后被人社局给停发了，完全靠家人帮助生活。黎容好在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日和家人一起，去广州看望朋友，随后被抓被带回中山市，可能是她近一段时间关注了正在狱中绝食抗争的公民记者张展的安危。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，黎容好女士的家人收到公安的刑事拘留通知书，称黎容好因涉嫌寻衅滋事罪被刑事拘留，现羁押在中山市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_64.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/11/blog-post_64.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黎芸：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">成都市新都区法轮功学员，女士，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">50</span>多岁。因坚持修炼法轮功，被中共当局多次关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日黎芸被成都市公安局新都区分局桂湖派出所抓捕，关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多；后于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被成都市新都区法院枉判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447879.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/8/20/447879.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黎智英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1948</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，英文名<span lang="EN-US">Jimmy Lai Chee-ying</span>，生于中国广州市，祖籍广东省顺德市，现为香港永久性居民，佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>）集团公司老板，香港《苹果日报》、壹传媒及《壹周刊》创办人，香港知名商人，香港民主派政党及组织的重要资助者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年，曾因生活穷困而被迫随广东发生的大规模“逃港潮”，借道澳门逃亡香港谋生，后经努力拼搏，于<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年创办了连锁服装品牌佐丹奴（<span lang="EN-US">Giordano</span>），并迅速使之成为当时风靡中港台的主要时装品牌之一；<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年，曾因同情天安门民主运动中的抗议学生，其旗下的佐丹奴印制了大量印有民运口号的<span lang="EN-US">T</span>恤供人们游行抗议时穿着，其本人也发表公开信敦促时任中国总理的李鹏下台谢罪，遂遭到六四镇压之后北京对香港商人的首批整肃，佐丹奴集团公司在中国大陆的全部业务被当局封杀，致其公司损失惨重，被迫低价出售股权；自此，其弃商从文，转而投身传媒事业，先后创办了壹传媒、《壹周刊》和《苹果日报》，但又因时常抨击中共时弊而被中国大陆禁止入境，其经手的报刊书籍亦被列入黑名单；长期以来，曾因其是香港民主运动（如香港雨伞运动、香港“反送中”抗议活动等）的重要支持者和资助商，故备受北京当局及香港建制派的批评、斥责，甚至指控其捐款为黑金；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因与美国副总统彭斯及美国国务卿蓬佩奥委会面，谈及香港现状及未来前途等事宜，而遭到中共当局的极度仇视和要打击的对象；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被香港警方以涉嫌“非法集结罪”抓捕，后被释放；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被以触犯香港《国安法》，涉嫌“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”及“串谋欺诈及煽动罪”拘捕，后暂获保释；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又被指控“欺诈罪”而收监逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天后，再被加控“勾结外国或者境外势力危害国家安全罪”被庭审；后其虽暂获保释，但<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日再度被捕，关押于香港荔枝角收押所，后与同案民主派高层领袖李卓人被香港西九龙裁判法院就<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8.18</span>维园“六四集会案”及<span lang="EN-US">8.31</span>“港岛游行案”进行宣判，其二人同时被判刑期<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年；之后很快其持有的壹传媒公司股份（市值超过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>亿元港币）及对其他三家公司在香港银行账户内所拥有的财产均被香港国安局冻结；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又被香港西九龙法院就其<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年“港岛游行案”和<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四集会案”数次庭审宣判，刑期共计<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，再被以其名下的力高公司涉嫌违反与特区政府香港科技园公司订立的地契为由，被特区高等法院以“欺诈罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">200</span>万港元（<span lang="EN-US">25.69</span>万美元<span lang="EN-US">/179</span>万元人民币），取消担任公司董事资格<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年；另有“勾结外国势力危害国家安全罪”案将推迟<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月（<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日）再审。目前在香港赤柱监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/59.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/59.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉长年：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉长年<span lang="EN-US">:</span>河南省人，基督徒，原河南“中华福音团契”（中国五大家庭教会之一）老一辈牧者，西安丰盛基督教教会创建人，主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年代末<span lang="EN-US">-1980</span>年代初起，因笃信基督教，即开始全职服侍教会；<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年，“中华福音团契”在河南省南阳市唐河县成立，故其曾长期在该教会进行司职；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后又因该教会发展壮大，成为拥有一千万多信众、数百名教牧团队、数十个对外宣教差会的最具规模的中国家庭教会，故而几十年来，其作为教会颇具影响力的神职人员，曾屡遭逼迫；曾因秉承基督信仰而被中共当局多次抓捕、拘禁和遭殴打；<span lang="EN-US">1991</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，曾以“中华福音团契”差传者的身份到湖北省襄阳市和襄樊市发展教会，而被湖北省警方以非法传教为由拘捕，后被判囚<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；获释后，因又到陕西省进行宣教活动，自此其就在西安市建立了丰盛基督教教会；但自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月中共新《宗教事务条例》正式生效实施起，全国各地基督教家庭教会纷纷遭遇空前严打和迫害，其所建西安丰盛教会亦遭严打和冲击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，自<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日始，其教会信徒突遭西安市灞桥区十里铺派出所警方大规模口头传唤和上门问讯，甚至有些人家被多次搜查，旨在胁迫信徒们作证，控告牧师诈骗和传播邪教，甚至要求信徒捏造有关教会奉献的虚假信息；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其及妻子、儿子廉旭亮、儿媳以及教会同工等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被当地派出所警方强行带走并被抄家，次日，其父子二人和教会财务同工付娟等人被西安市灞桥区警方以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其教会被西安市民政局迅速发布通告取缔，理由是其与“中华福音总会”、“中华福音总会”西安区联会，“未经登记”就擅自以社会团体名义开展活动，故被认定为非法社会组织；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被指定居所监视居住长达半年之久的西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道被以涉嫌诈骗罪的名义刑事拘留，羁押到看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道的代理律师获准分别会见了当事人。据他们三人的口述，在指定监视居住期间，他们都受到不同程度的虐待和刑讯逼供。审讯人员用廉长年牧师的儿子廉旭亮牧师来威胁他，并且共有七八次殴打廉旭亮牧师，甚至当着廉长年的牧师的面殴打。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">廉旭亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省人，基督徒，西安丰盛基督教教会主任牧师廉长年之长子，西安丰盛基督教教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。廉旭亮自其父亲廉长年牧师在陕西省建立“西安丰盛基督教教会”以来，因笃信基督教，其及妻子亦投身于教会的传教与服侍活动；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年秋，其被按立为牧师，但因时逢中共新《宗教事务条例》开始实施，全国各地基督教家庭教会纷纷遭遇空前打压和逼迫，故其所在西安丰盛教会亦遭多次严打和冲击；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日开始，因其教会及其本人一直不愿意接受中共“三自教会”的管控，遂其教会的聚会活动频遭冲击，大批教友突遭西安市灞桥区十里铺派出所警方多次传唤和质询，甚至部分女性教友遭到辱骂和恐吓，部分男性教遭到辱骂、恐吓和殴打，一些教友家里被搜查；后从被获释的教友那里得知，警方此番打压行动旨在胁迫信徒们作伪证，以控告教会牧师诈骗和传播邪教，以及要求他们捏造有关教会奉献的虚假信息；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，其父及其夫妇二人、其<span lang="EN-US">9</span>岁的儿子以及教会其他同工、传道等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被当地派出所警方强行带走和抄家；后其<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被释放，但次日（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日），廉旭亮及其父亲廉长年牧师、教会财务同工付娟<span lang="EN-US">3</span>人又被西安市灞桥区警方抓走，并被以涉嫌“诈骗罪”指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，其教会被西安市民政局迅速发布通告取缔，理由是其与“中华福音总会”、“中华福音总会”西安区联会，“未经登记”就擅自以社会团体名义开展活动，故被认定为非法社会组织；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被指定居所监视居住长达半年之久的西安丰盛教会的廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道被以涉嫌诈骗罪的名义刑事拘留，羁押到看守所。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日上午，廉长年牧师、廉旭亮牧师、付娟传道的代理律师获准分别会见了当事人。据他们三人的口述，在指定监视居住期间，他们都受到不同程度的虐待和刑讯逼供。审讯人员用廉长年牧师的儿子廉旭亮牧师来威胁他，并且共有七八次殴打廉旭亮牧师，甚至当着廉长年的牧师的面殴打。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_39.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp;</span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/blog-post_18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">练日光：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省惠州市博罗县法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月出生，家住阳春市春城镇<span lang="EN-US">9</span>头坡村。练日光<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年毕业于阳江师范学院，毕业后在阳春市春湾镇卫国乡小学教书，<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年调到合水镇平北小学，<span lang="EN-US">1992</span>年调到营讯小学。因为修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，他被阳春市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，被关押到阳江监狱迫害，随后他被开除公职。从监狱黑窝出来后，阳春市公安局将他列入管控对象，合水镇综治信访维稳中心对他长期监控和骚扰。练日光在灵泉学堂教数学。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">11</span>时左右，博罗县公安局国保大队几乎倾巢出动，和九潭派出所警察一块，以查经营为由，从邻居家闯入灵泉学堂，查抄。查抄中，发现有法轮功书籍，警察将赵天华抓捕，他的妻子蔡惠斌、灵泉学堂的教师陈华良、练日光一起被抓捕，被关押到博罗县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被惠州市惠城区法院判决：练日光被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/9/451690.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁春华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林市龙潭区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，在吉林市大华市场与商家兑换真相币时，被警察跟踪绑架，<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元左右真相币被警察抢走，梁春华先被行政拘留十天。三月二十七日拘留到期，警察直接将梁春华拉走，抄家，抢走工资卡、存折等物品，家里被劫的空荡荡。然后将梁春华又劫持到吉林市看守所关押，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，被关押在吉林省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁顺景<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，广东省梅州市梅县区城东镇人，原中国工商银行梅州分行职工，梅州城区江南团结路苏泊尔电器店负责人，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。因为人谦和、厚道而深受他人好评；又因其与其妻邓秀芬在当地共同承办苏泊尔电器店（主营电器厨器专卖批发），生意上注重诚实守信，随其公司至<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年底时已有较大发展；但因梁顺景、邓秀芬夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在信仰追求上笃信并积极宣传法轮功，随遭广东省梅州市当局的强力打压；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人在开车外出讲解宣传法轮功时，被事先蹲坑等候的梅州市梅江区警方及“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”管理办公室人员联合抓走，其家遭查抄，当场搜走法轮功书籍多套、计算机、打印机及银行卡、身份证等个人对象（如）多件，并将其日用汽车也拉走扣留；次日，其妻因血压高达<span lang="EN-US">180/230</span>，让家人暂时接回，其本人则被梅江区警方以涉嫌邪教罪刑拘，关押至梅江区芹黄看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，其夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人被梅江区检察院以同罪名正式批捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在梅州市梅江区法院开庭审理；虽因该法院违反法定诉讼程序，其辩护律师曾据理要求法院重新开庭审判，但其与其妻仍然被该法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”枉法重判；其中<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">，梁顺景被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，其妻邓秀芬被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，并各处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；其<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人不服，均提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，经广东省梅州市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；其刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其妻邓秀芬刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日；</b>据悉，其在看守所时被查出身体长有<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个肿瘤，在被庭审时其辩护权及辩护律师执业权被剥夺；其承办的苏泊尔电器店因长时无人经营，故被迫关门。目前在广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱（广东省<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会市济广塘镇<span lang="EN-US">/</span>广东省肇庆市<span lang="EN-US">4</span>会监狱<span lang="EN-US">290</span>信箱，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">526237</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">梁琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">基督徒，云南省临沧市云县基督教传道人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年因在云南省多地<span lang="EN-US">/</span>州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>市传道和发展信徒，随被当局以涉嫌“参与三班仆人派邪教组织”为罪由抓捕，其住处所在地遭查抄，搜走传道宣传品<span lang="EN-US">1831</span>份、传单<span lang="EN-US">2556</span>份，并从电子设备中提取到的电子文件<span lang="EN-US">82816</span>个等。后被云南省临沧市云县检察院宣布正式批捕，并被指控其一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人是邪教骨干分子，“到云南省多地州市秘密聚会、传经布道和发展信徒，继续鼓吹、宣扬世界末日论，培养组织骨干，为秘密传教布道聚会创造条件和提供便利，重建‘三班仆人派’组织体系等”。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人分别被云南省临沧市云县法院以“组织利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月到<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等。其中，鞠殿红因是要犯，被重判<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年；<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">梁琴因是要犯被重判<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</b>其余<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人，具体刑期不详。但此<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人都因不服判决，都已提起上诉。梁琴刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市丰台区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年代生人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，梁新在北京东城区亮果厂胡同发法轮功资料时，被监控器监控；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，梁新被东城区石景山派出所抓捕、抄家，许多私人物品被抢劫。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，梁新被北京东城区公安分局非法拘留。关押在北京市东城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">梁耀敏：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，山东海阳市法轮功学员。其原本是海阳市公安局刑警队痕迹检验工程师，技术精湛，经她鉴定破获了许多大案、要案，是全省少有的女性侦察技术人员。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日中共江开始疯狂迫害法轮功，梁耀敏仅仅因为坚持自己的信仰、继续修炼法轮功，经历了被关押、开除公职、关洗脑班、关精神病院、劳教、判刑、停发退休金等种种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年曾被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，在山东省女子监狱遭受关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，山东海阳市国保警察共抓捕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>名法轮功学员：梁耀敏、张俊峰、张吉国、王成刚、纪力骁、隋伟丽、于海勇和王雪梅夫妻。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，梁耀敏与另外几位女法轮功学员被关押到烟台牟平看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，梁耀敏被批捕，同时由烟台牟平看守所转押到烟台福山看守所。年逾<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁的法轮功学员梁耀敏，被抓捕、关押在烟台市看守所，由于长期的被关押迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在被海阳市（凤城）法院的视频庭审期间，当庭出现严重的心绞痛情况，生命垂危，看守所怕出事当场实施紧急抢救。梁耀敏<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日再次被开庭，公诉方捏造伪证的行径再次被曝光。辩护律师依法逐条说明了公诉方提供的各项所谓人证、物证均无法律效力，要求当庭释放。但是最终梁耀敏被枉判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/1/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%B5%B7%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%A2%81%E8%80%80%E6%95%8F%E7%AD%89%E5%9B%9B%E4%BD%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-440738.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 351.75pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">梁子亮：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广东鹤山市沙坪街道浸信教会传道人，梁子亮与妻子李银秀，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日带领信徒在当地一公园内拉横幅反对堕胎以及传福音，当晚被警察传唤到派出所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，梁子亮与妻子李银秀的家属，接到鹤山市公安局发出的刑事拘留通知书，两份通知书分别指梁子梁和李银秀，违反刑事诉讼法第八十条之规定，涉嫌组织、资助非法聚集罪，刑事拘留，现羁押在鹤山市看守所。据信徒介绍，梁子亮原是当地官办三自教会的信徒，后离开“三自”，成立家庭教会。目前，浸信教会有信徒约二十人。每周举行聚会，梁子亮还会带领信徒外出传福音，也因此多次受到警察警告。广东省基督教因传福音被刑事拘留的案子，并不多见。很多教会担心当局此举是为了震慑其他家庭教会，以阻止信徒外出传福音。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林春子：黑龙江</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">牡丹江市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年已经<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁，朝鲜族，在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，她被牡丹江市公检法暗箱操作判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，因身体原因监外执行。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，林春子到外寄信，被警察秘密抓捕。家人和朋友经多方查询，证实林春子已被抓捕到黑龙江省哈尔滨女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457348.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/3/457348.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林大卫：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1955</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，祖籍不详，美籍华人，英文名<span lang="EN-US">David Lin</span>，美国爱荷华州（<span lang="EN-US">Iowa</span>）和加利福尼亚州（<span lang="EN-US">California</span>）经济顾问，基督徒，美国基督复临安息日会牧师，针对中国家庭教会的宣道士，中国在押良心犯。自移民美国以来，早期曾专注于养家糊口，并自己熟知的领域一直努力工作；后入籍成为美国公民，曾在爱荷华州和加利福尼亚州担任政府官员的经济顾问；来美之初，其并无基督信仰，并认为只有无知的人才会信教，但多年之后，当其妻子成为基督徒后，其开始深入了解基督教信仰；后其受洗成为基督徒，并自此开始积极参与教会的服事活动；<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，因其经常到中国旅行，期间深刻感受到基督教福音在中国广传的必要性，遂立定心志，以期能从中国官方最终获得开始基督教事工的许可；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年，已是教会牧师的他开始了中国大陆差传宣道之旅；此期间，因中国政府为成功申办<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年奥运会，曾一度营造“外松”形象，故而一时吸引了众多基督教工作者来华倡导，但实因中共本质上的思想意识倾向与基督教宣传的价值取向完全相左，遂在<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年前后启动的一项代号为“台风五号”秘密行动中，数以百计的外国来华传教士被驱逐；其亦在此打压行动中，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年，因帮助中国家庭教会盖一座教堂而被中国警方突然拘押和被禁止离境；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，其被中国某检察院以涉嫌“合同诈骗罪”予以批捕，指控其因“合同欺诈”而触犯了中国相关法律，故而应予逮捕、重判；随后其案很快被检察院起诉，并将其案宗移交至中国某法院审查；同年，终被中国某法院以“合同诈骗罪”枉法重判无期徒刑；据悉，被判之初，其家人尚选择保持沉默和低调处事，因其表明已将监狱视为施教、分享信仰和鼓励来自<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多个国家的囚犯的机会，故其在狱中建立了每周一次的礼拜天祷告会，并致力于将圣经译成中文；但时至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2019</span>年初，其在与家人的定期电话中突然明确要求帮助其尽早获得释放；后从官方得知其健康状况正在恶化，疑指可能“遭非人道虐待”等，遂开始寻求美国拜登总统及政府的帮助，以期能被无罪释放；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月获悉，其已被中共当局执行减刑，但刑期仍需至<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。目前服刑监狱不详。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/david-lin_15.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/david-lin_15.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林闺臣</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：福州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1960</span>年生，系福建省农科院耕作所退休女职工。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在发法轮功资料时，被福州市公安局鼓楼区温泉派出所警察抓捕到明清县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被批捕。马尾区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月对她庭审，后对她判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/9/450587.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林国兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林省通化市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，家住吉林省通化市东昌区。自<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年林国兰开始修炼法轮功以来，受益良多。林国兰<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日去通化县江沿等地发放法轮功资料，被通化县公安局国保大队警察抓捕、构陷，后悉已经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初被送进吉林省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/27/450144.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/27/450144.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林乐宏：女，</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，大学本科毕业，家住深圳市南山区。林乐宏和马彦平都暂在深圳龙岗区布吉镇大芬油画村租住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日晚上，林乐宏、马彦平在大芬油画村租住房内，被龙岗区公安分局国保及布吉派出所警察抓捕，并被抄家，两人被关押到龙岗区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，警察再次对<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人的租住房进行了查抄，将法轮功书籍、资料、电脑、打印机、塑封机、切边机、硬盘、<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘等个人物品全部劫走。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，林乐宏、马彦平被龙岗区检察院批捕。被关押后，林乐宏多次绝食反迫害，遭看守所强制灌食，健康受到严重伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，林乐宏被强制灌食后，被送医院所谓“抢救”。从此，林乐宏吃什么吐什么，回到看守所后，身体<span lang="EN-US">1</span>直不好。血压高至<span lang="EN-US">160/180mmHg</span>（低血压高）。她每周需要吸氧<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次，只能吃流食，出现心口痛，左手麻木。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，林乐宏、马彦平被盐田区法院庭审。有律师出庭做无罪辩护。为了抵制持续的迫害，从<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日始，林乐宏又开始绝食，被连续强制灌食<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多天。体重只剩<span lang="EN-US">46</span>公斤，舌根发硬，吞咽困难，胸口时常发闷，血糖极低（不到<span lang="EN-US">3mmol/L</span>），手脚冰凉，特别怕冷，<span lang="EN-US">26</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">︒</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">C</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">的气温下还要穿大棉袄。在林乐宏身体健康严重受损的情况下，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，盐田区法院宣判，林乐宏被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；马彦平被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，被罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">刑期至：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/28/%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E6%9E%97%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%8F%E3%80%81%E9%A9%AC%E5%BD%A6%E5%B9%B3%E5%A5%B3%E5%A3%AB%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%A4%9A-440593.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林丽红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">沈阳市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月生，家住辽宁省沈阳市沈河区东陵路。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，林丽红在沈河区富友小区东门被警察抓捕，并被抄家。警察抄走她的大法书、大法法像及手机等。林丽红被关押在沈阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林丽红被经济技术开发区法院分别判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/12/458715.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/12/458715.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林久良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">另名林素梁，<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">四川</span>成都市新津区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生，女，家住成都市新津区<span lang="EN-US">5</span>津街道。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年修炼法轮功。她却因为坚持修炼，遭受中共当局的种种迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被大邑县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。林久良<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午向世人讲法轮功，被成都市大邑县公安局沙渠派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被成都市大邑县法院视频开庭、判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446034.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/10/446034.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林立盛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东省茂名市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日再次抓捕林立盛。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月获悉茂南区公检法合谋对林立盛判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/3/454462.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/3/454462.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">林茂成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">大连市金州区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，林茂成给陌生人讲法轮功，被他诬告后遭抓捕抄家，非法拿走大法书籍、计算机、打印机、身份证、驾驶证等物品。林茂成被劫持到派出所期间强制照相，录指纹、声音、验血、做完笔录后，逼他签字未果。半夜后，人被放回，监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，林茂成被大连普兰店检察院批捕，并被大连大孤山边防派出所强制关押在大连开发区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，林茂成被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林明洁：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">是辽宁省沈阳市铁西区人，原辽宁省某国企技术人员，人称“访民义侠”，维权公民，人权捍卫者，曾获得海外中国民主党颁发的曹顺利勇气奖。早年因不服其兄林明华被行政拘留和家里拆迁补偿的问题而走上信访之路，后因长期到京上访，并热心为访民维权发声而屡遭当局非法绑架、关押、拘留等打击迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁因在北京国家信访局、住建部反映地方政府违法强拆事宜，被沈阳市驻京办等截访人员跟踪骚扰，后被强行遣返原籍，并被沈阳市铁西区警方予以刑事拘留，一个月后才得以释放；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，又因和一批沈阳访民在中国公安部六部口信访局集体上访（简称“集访”），状告沈阳市公安局与局长许文有徇私枉法，随后被沈阳市截访人员抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日被沈阳市铁西区警方以涉嫌“扰乱公共场所秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区检察院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”正式批捕，并控诉其罪状：在北京多次集访扰乱公共秩序、在庆安徐纯合案时打出“我是访民，朝我开枪”的标语、长期将访民维权的新闻发给境外媒体等。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，林明洁被沈阳市铁西区法院一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日止。此前曾被羁押于沈阳市铁西区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，林明洁结束两年多的监狱生活刑满获释。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年十一前，与哥哥林明华一起遭警方抓捕，据悉已被刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日律师会见才获悉：林明洁被以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，“非法利用信息网络罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，合并执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。林明洁的兄长林明华被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">林武：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东茂名市电白区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，原广州远洋轮公司职工，他是一个很有经验的船员、水手。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年前，林武与妻子李素真开始修炼法轮功后，双双身心受益。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，中共江泽民团伙迫害法轮功后，林武因坚修炼法轮功，被单位取消提工资资格；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，林武在家中被茂名市高新技术公安分局警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日上午，在看守所里林武被茂名市茂南区法院宣判。他被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚金一万五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/1/%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%85%B3%E6%8A%BC%E4%B8%A4%E5%B9%B4%E5%90%8E-%E9%80%80%E4%BC%91%E6%B5%B7%E5%91%98%E6%9E%97%E6%AD%A6%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-463641.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; minor-fareast;">浙江省温州市人，基督徒，浙江省温州某归正家庭教会同工，四川省泸州市古蔺县受邀差传倡导者（即受原教会派遣，跨区域给未信者广传福音的基督徒），中国在押良心犯。因笃信耶稣基督，而致力于广传基督教福音并积极参与教会的服事活动，遂深受教会牧者及教友们的喜爱与信任；近年来，因受邀到四川省泸州市古蔺县某一偏远山区看望基督徒，虽欣然前往，但却发现该地区不仅属国家级特困县，而且民众的信仰也甚荒凉，遂决定留在古蔺县，以期用热心、爱心和耐心给未信者传讲福音；然而，自中共当局开始对宗教自由信仰越发严苛的打压之后，其传播基督教活动，如礼拜天聚会、唱赞美诗、查考研读圣经等，引起四川管理者当局的不悦与警戒；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其与另两位基督徒被泸州市古蔺县警方以是“有社会危险性”人员为由，以涉嫌“组织、资助非法聚集罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，另两位基督徒被准予取保候审，但其仍被扣押，并被古蔺县警方以同罪名正式逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其案被古蔺县警方提交至古蔺县检察院审查起诉；已有律师介入。目前被羁押于四川古蔺县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; lang="EN-US">15</span>日，林炎德在使用真相基站发送信息时，被揭阳市公安局空港分局国保和渔湖派出所警察蹲守抓捕，关押到揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，法院到揭阳市看守所宣判，林炎德被判重刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，他被关押到广东省四会监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江鸡西市密山法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月生。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下，林永霞从外面回到她的住处，被蹲坑的密山市公安局国保警察抓捕，抄家，抄走法轮功书籍和个人物品等。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月得知她已经被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2023/8/1/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E9%B8%A1%E8%A5%BF%E5%B8%82%E5%AF%86%E5%B1%B1%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%9E%97%E6%B0%B8%E9%9C%9E%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-463649.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">林在务：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日出生，化名林大海、林忠，福建省福清市人，福清市东瀚镇东瀚村田尾<span lang="EN-US">17</span>号村民，“耶和华见证人”宗教团体信徒，新疆“耶和华见证人”长老和管理人，中国在押良心犯。因信仰耶和华见证人教派，并被委任在新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州（简称巴音州）库尔勒地区做教会长老，在库尔勒市组成家庭聚会，举行上百次大型聚会及成员培训，大力发展信徒，随遭极左思维极强的中共新疆当局严打狠批；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，在“耶和华见证人案”大抓捕中，被库尔勒市警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”与多人先后刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被以涉嫌“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”转正式逮捕，指控其与教会多名长老和信徒因打着基督教旗号，组织会众聚会，宣扬“政治中立，蛊惑、煽动耶和华见证人会众及他人不履行公民法定义务，如不入党<span lang="EN-US">/</span>团，不服兵役，不升国旗，不向国旗敬礼，不唱国歌，不参加选举等，并与境外人员定期聚会，借机敛财，影响群众正常宗教信仰，扰乱社会秩序，破坏了国家的法律法规，故而其等行为已构成违法；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人涉邪教案被警方向库尔勒市检察院提起公诉；后<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被检察院发回补帧，但同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月又被补查重报；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，其等被库尔勒市法院一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”统一判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月至<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月不等刑期，其中，其被重判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；其等不服，均表上诉；后经巴音郭楞蒙古自治州中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日；据悉，曾因在看守所内拒唱“红歌”等，常遭狱警连体铐、抱铐等体罚虐待。目前在新疆生产建设兵团农二师监狱（新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市建国南路<span lang="EN-US">15</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">841000</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/66_24.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/66_24.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;
