mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/19/453295.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘晓红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生。大连市第四人民医院护士，因修炼法轮大法，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被沙河口区白山路派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月初，她被甘井子区法院一审判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，她上诉，二审维持违法原判；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，她被大连市卫生健康委员会违法开除公职。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/21/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%8A%A4%E5%A3%AB%E5%88%98%E6%99%93%E7%BA%A2%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E3%80%81%E5%BC%80%E9%99%A4%E5%85%AC%E8%81%8C%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-440300.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/21/%E5%A4%A7%E8%BF%9E%E6%8A%A4%E5%A3%AB%E5%88%98%E6%99%93%E7%BA%A2%E9%81%AD%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4%E3%80%81%E5%BC%80%E9%99%A4%E5%85%AC%E8%81%8C%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-440300.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘晓慧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省济南市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年生，家住济南天桥区黄屯小区六区。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日早上七点多，在家中被天桥区公安国保大队和无影山派出所警察抓捕，后遭刑事拘留，被关押到济南看守所。刘晓慧被关押一年六个月后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，被济南市天桥区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘小妙：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1949</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，河北省深泽县东北留村。因为修炼法轮功，自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">720</span>后被中共当局多次关押迫害，遭受酷刑。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日石家庄市深泽县十多名法轮功学员半夜被突然抓捕，其中何红彦、刘小妙、杜国防等八人一直被关押在石家庄市第二看守所和晋州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被构陷到晋州市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在晋州市法院被开庭，据<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，把人均已被判刑。刘小妙被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘星：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25-27</span>日，刘星、刘玉红、董秀荣、靳书英等法轮功学员被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉：刘玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刘星<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，董秀荣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，靳书英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刘星刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘兴国</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：河南省潢川县白店乡白店村的农民，生于<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年，今年已经整整<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁了。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，国家<span lang="EN-US">1704</span>粮食储备库建到了白店乡白店村，根据刘兴国获取的该粮食储备库的审计表显示，给予集体经济组织的补偿总共才<span lang="EN-US">350</span>余万人民币（失地农民并没有足额拿到这些补偿），却给白店乡政府征地的奖励达<span lang="EN-US">50</span>万人民币，加上给参与征地的派出所<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万、媒体<span lang="EN-US">9</span>万元人民币。更令刘兴国感到不安的，是该<span lang="EN-US">1704</span>国家粮食储备库自从建成后，居然没有储存<span lang="EN-US">1</span>斤可食用的粮食，而是收进只能用于工业的陈化粮以套取国家补助而中饱私囊。当年“三面红旗”时期差一点被饿死的刘兴国，就同村民徐耀辉、王国强、王金国、蔡金芳、陈德琴、郑庆梅等，向国家机关及国内媒体投诉举报，还持证据材料到北京有关部门信访反映。正因为刘兴国的进京信访行为，遭来了地方官吏的疯狂打压，在刘兴国遭到暴力截访后，多次被处以治安拘留，还在白店乡派出所对其实施酷刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年年全国“两会”期间，刘兴国在北京再次遭到潢川县公安局驻京的刘桂红等人的截访，到<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日（农历<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初二）被以“涉嫌寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，到<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被批捕。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">刘秀英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">广州市花都区法轮功学员。刘秀英<span lang="EN-US">1948</span>年出生，湖南省洪江市人，家住广州市花都区新华街横谭村。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被广州市公安局花都区分局警察抓捕，关押到花都区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被荔湾区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/27/2022-1-27.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘秀云：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，北京丰台区玉泉营派出所六、七人闯入刘秀云（女，六十多岁）家中，将其抓捕至玉泉营派出所，并抄走大法书籍。原因是因监控看到发真相资料，跟踪到家。<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午， 刘秀云遭刑事拘留，现被关押在北京丰台区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，刘秀云被丰台法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘学刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘学刚因坚持修炼法轮功曾多次遭受迫害，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月他被关押<span lang="EN-US">48</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年被劳教二年；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被鸡冠区国保抓捕，被鸡冠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年刑。刘学刚<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被恒山区小恒山派出所警察闯入在鸡东县的家中抄家、抓捕、构陷。后得知，他被鸡东县法院判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源<span lang="EN-US">:</span></b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458685.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/11/458685.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘艳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">云南省昆明市法轮功学员。女，毕业于东北师范大学。研究生毕业后，到空军航空大学做外语教官。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，刘艳被迫复原，离开部队后，刘艳在中国和加拿大联合办学的莱姆顿学院做外事办主任。教学期间，因长春警察多次抓捕刘艳，她在长春实在无法正常生活，于<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年和丈夫带着女儿到云南。曾任云南文理学院大学外语教学部主任、副教授，因坚持修炼法轮功多次遭中共迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，她在自己家的工厂门口，被昆明市公安局五华分局、海源寺派出所、黑林铺派出所一众警察抓捕，被关押在昆明市看守所。警方不让她家属接见，甚至律师也被拒绝探视。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，当地法院对刘艳进行庭审。<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月后，对刘艳判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元。刑期至：<a name="_Hlk101728734"><span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk101728734;"></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/22/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E5%A5%B3%E5%89%AF%E6%95%99%E6%8E%88%E5%88%98%E8%89%B3%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441589.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk101728734;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/22/%E4%BA%91%E5%8D%97%E5%A5%B3%E5%89%AF%E6%95%99%E6%8E%88%E5%88%98%E8%89%B3%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-441589.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk101728734;"></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/36_18.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/05/36_18.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> <o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘艳（河北）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北省承德市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年左右生，女。其于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被承德市公安局双桥分局政保大队警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，家属收到逮捕通知书，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，承德市双桥区法院对其判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458755.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458755.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖北省武穴市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1964</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月出生，家住武穴市城区，现在被非法关押在黄冈市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日凌晨，武穴市公安局、田镇派出所、青林派出所、龙潭派出所同时出动，同一时间对郭平珍、龚月贵、刘艳峰、程学珍和廖元华五位法轮功学员的住宅、工作场所、法轮功学员及家人租借的房屋与仓库进行非法查抄，抄走法轮功书籍、资料、打印机、电脑等个人物品，并将五位法轮功学员抓捕，关押到看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，这五位法轮功学员被武穴市检察院非法批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，武穴市法院将五位法轮功学员判刑。郭平珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；龚月贵、刘艳峰和程学珍被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元；廖元华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。刘艳峰刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘艳华<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南周口市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被中共劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，之后多次被骚扰。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，刘艳华及丈夫刘冲还有到她家串门的法轮功学员杜子良，被河南省周口市公安局荷花分局四、五个警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年元月，刘艳华被河南周口市川汇区法院第三刑事庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，家属毫不知情。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘燕美</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东东营胜利油田法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，山东省东营地区滨海公安局出动大量警力，一天之内，肆意抓捕了刘燕美等二十多位胜利油田的法轮功学员。后刘燕美被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，被罚金五万。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/24/462293.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/24/462293.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘彦学：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西省九江市城子镇法轮功学员。刘彦学于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，被九江市柴桑区公安局抓捕，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/19/461016.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/5/19/461016.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘尧：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广东河源市知名维权律师。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1961</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生。刘尧是自学成为律师，曾专门受理农民与开发商及地方官员间的“征地”纠纷案件。刘尧第一次出名是在</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2007</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月，当时他因参与一场农村抗议活动被拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2008</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，刘尧被判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑。此前，刘尧所代表的村民与一个水电站的保安人员对峙，检方称，有价值</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">5</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币的建筑材料在对峙中被毁坏。对这个情节较轻的案件，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年的结果在中国法律界引起抗议。法律人士纷纷为他辩护。当时是李方平和浦志强等维权律师代理他进行了一系列上诉，最终使刘尧的刑期减为</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">16</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">个月监禁。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-language: ZH-TW; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月下旬，刘尧实名向中共广东省纪检委举报，并在网上发文，指河源市委书记何忠友非法支持广东康泉十八国际生态健康旅游城有限公司违法占用农地，包括基本农田的项目，修建高尔夫球场。中国的法规（基本农田保护条例第</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">15</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">17</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">条）明确规定任何单位和个人不得改变或者占用基本农田。同时，刘尧还向纪检委举报当时河源市公安局局长彭定邦毫无理由地停止调查</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名商人销售假冒著名韶关钢铁公司品牌的钢材，敦促纪委以涉嫌受贿的问题调查彭定邦。没多久，于</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2015</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">12</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被河源市公安局源城分局以涉嫌“为境外非法提供国家秘密罪”（后撤销指控）和“敲诈勒索罪”刑事拘留。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2017</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">4</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日，刘尧被广东河源市源城区法院以“敲诈勒索罪”、“诈骗罪”和“收买被拐卖的儿童罪”数罪并罚，判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">20</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑，罚金</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">140</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">万元人民币（</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">221,000</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">美元）。刘尧认为，他被起诉和定罪，是因为他长期举报河源市党政官员的贪腐行为，而遭到河源市</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">60</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">多名纪检、检察、法院官员“帮助腐败党政高官报复陷害”。后上诉、申诉均遭驳回。刑期至：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2036</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">24</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘跃丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省广州法轮功学员，女，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">住广州市番禺区祈福新邨。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中旬，被番禺区屏山派出所抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，广州法轮功学员刘跃丽被广州市海珠区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。目前仍被关押在番禺区看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/10/451702.html"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">刘义波<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">湖北孝感市汉川市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，肖艳芳、刘义波、王四美、王庆、舒运兰等<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人到汉川市马鞍乡联洪村、天成村告诉村民法轮功遭迫害真相及避疫良方，被村民举报，遭马鞍派出所警察抓捕。第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人因疫情原因被放回家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，汉川市公安局对肖艳芳、刘义波、王庆、王四美、舒运兰<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人下达「监视居住通知书」。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日肖艳芳、刘义波被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，汉川国保人员到湖南长沙，将流落在外打工的法轮功学员王庆抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，汉川市公安局分水派出所警察在分水镇抓捕了王四美和另一名法轮功学员胡汉姣。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月下旬，孝昌县法院作出判决，胡汉姣、王四美遭判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刘义波遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，肖艳芳遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，王庆遭判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刘义波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 141.95pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘一涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; 0pt;">原江西省广播电视大学教师。刘一涛于<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年被抓捕、遭判刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年后，在江西省女子监狱，刘一涛被关押迫害<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年后，于<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年初出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，刘一涛向快递员讲法轮功，被恶意构陷抓捕，后被关押在南昌市第一看守所。期间，刘一涛多次遭同监号被关押人员辱骂、殴打。公检法暗箱操作、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年（具体时间不详），刘一涛再被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现已被送往省女子监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/23/457054.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日去黄旗赶集买鸡蛋，回家途中被红旗派出所抓捕抄家。于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日被凤城法院庭审，后获悉刘银凤被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘友</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：男，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，辽宁锦州市太和区流水村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日晚上，刘友在家中被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被送到锦州市看守所关押。刘友被抄家两次，警察抄走打印机、电脑、法轮功书籍等私人物品。警察让刘友的两个女儿劝说刘友“咬出（即出卖）三个人来”。刘友说这些都是自己的东西。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月获悉，其已被锦州凌海法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，现在仍被关押在锦州市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">，女，<span lang="EN-US">1959</span>年生，济南市长清区归德镇董庄人，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被济南市公安局长清分局归德派出所抓捕，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日回家。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，刘玉桂又被抓捕送到济南市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，刘玉桂的家人突然接到济南市长清区法院判决书，刘玉桂被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/10/454720.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">刘玉红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">北京法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25-27</span>日，刘星、刘玉红、董秀荣、靳书英等法轮功学员被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月获悉：刘玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刘星<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，董秀荣<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，靳书英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。刘玉红刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/13/458748.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘玉华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁铁岭市法轮功学员。刘玉华和丈夫靳利国都修炼法轮功。一九九九年七月二十日，中共开始迫害法轮功后，刘玉华和靳利国曾遭中共多次绑架、关押。由于此前靳利国和刘玉华夫妇往一些公检法部门邮寄了“明真相保平安”的劝善信，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，铁岭市昌图县国保大队封锁了靳利国和刘玉华夫妇家的楼道，谎称抓“杀人犯”，闯入靳利国和刘玉华夫妇家里，实施抓捕和抄家，后刘玉华被铁岭市昌图县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；丈夫靳利国被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，身体十分虚弱的刘玉华被转入辽宁省女子监狱迫害。据悉，在看守所非法关押期间，刘玉华被迫害得很严重，导致血压高达<span lang="EN-US">200mmHg</span>，糖代谢紊乱，血糖高达<span lang="EN-US">14mmol</span>／<span lang="EN-US">L</span>（空腹血糖正常值：<span lang="EN-US">3.9</span>～<span lang="EN-US">5.5mmol</span>／<span lang="EN-US">L</span>），骨瘦如柴。而且，刘玉华左臂麻木，左腿动不了，检查结果是腔隙性脑梗。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨市尚志市法轮功学员。女。<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日早上，刘玉梅在哈尔滨南岗区贵新街邮政银行旁边的小区家中被抓捕。警察对刘玉梅家抄家，抢走电脑笔记本，打印机，大法书籍等私人物品，还抢走了<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>多元现金，那是她仅有的生活费。后</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，狱中情况很惨，满口只剩<span lang="EN-US">1</span>颗牙齿。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/23/455939.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/23/455939.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">刘玉秋：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt;">黑龙江省鹤岗市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日刘玉秋在家被当地警察断电抓捕，关押在鹤岗市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月得知刘玉秋被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，已被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘玉茹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">石家庄市深泽县法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1968</span>年生，深泽县西南留村人，一九九八年修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日石家庄市深泽县十多名法轮功学员半夜被突然抓捕，其中刘玉茹等八人一直被关押在石家庄市第二看守所和晋州市看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日被构陷到晋州市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日在晋州市法院被开庭，据<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日获悉，把人均已被判刑。刘玉茹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/11/461862.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">刘增奎</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：哈尔滨市香坊区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>至<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，哈尔滨市、区三十多名法轮功学员被绑架，刘增奎于<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被香坊区警察抓捕、抄家、关押构陷。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日上午刘增奎被哈尔滨市道里区法院视频远程开庭，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘珍俐：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市东西湖区女法轮功学员。原武汉东西湖新沟镇棉纺织厂职工。仅仅因为法轮功学员的身份，刘珍俐曾经在<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕、关押在洗脑班；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，她被抓捕到何湾劳教所劳教；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，她被抓捕、判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日刘珍俐在自家门口被东西湖区吴家山街派出所抓捕、关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，获悉其于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刘志峰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，刘志峰等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，刘志峰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">柳德玉：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">湖北荆门市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，原是荆门市卫生防疫站干部，一九九六年开始修炼法轮功。在中共邪党对迫害法轮功的疯狂迫害中，他曾多次被抓捕、关押，累计被关押迫害长达<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年之久。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，柳德玉曾因给民众讲法轮功真相，被东宝区泉口派出所警察抓捕，当晚被放回。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，柳德玉在街头给百姓讲真相时，再次被东宝区泉口派出所警察抓捕，一直被关押在荆门看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月获悉，柳德玉被东宝区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，他目前仍被关押在荆门市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/15/456798.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/15/456798.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳木兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">武汉市新洲区法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生，武汉新洲区农家妇女，曾遭中共冤狱迫害三年半，被迫害致非常消瘦、精神恍惚。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日中午，在租住地，被便衣警察绑架，后一直被关押在武汉市第一看守所，看守所将不明药物偷偷放在她的饭里面。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月下旬才得知，柳木兰被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索四千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">柳秋生：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江西省九江市法轮功学员，都昌县人。柳秋生原来在都昌县调查队从事统计调查工作（公务员）。因为坚持信仰真善忍，遭迫害被开除公职，没有生活来源。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，柳秋生遭抓捕。非法抄家时抄收现金六万元还有存款和五万美元存单。构陷编造的罪名是“里通外国”，其实是柳秋生家中房屋拆迁款，柳秋生在银行的同学帮助存了美元存单，取不了，美元只是利息高点，这笔钱是留给儿子读大学用的。当局给柳秋生强按的罪名是“里通外国”，<span lang="EN-US"> 2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被九江市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳全春：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1975</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，辽宁省大石桥市旗口镇农民，法轮功学员。辽宁大石桥市法轮功学员柳全春、史庆秀夫妇，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被抓捕、构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日遭营口市站前区法院在看守所庭审，两位律师出庭为他们进行无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">第<span lang="EN-US">2</span>天，法官赵丹就下了判决：分别判刑柳全春和史庆秀<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元，并没收所有扣押的物品。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">柳涛：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">四川省绵阳市法轮功学员。柳涛女士，大学毕业后在深圳工作。在<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年七月江泽民迫害法轮功后，她讲法轮功真相，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，在广东三水劳教所因炼功被每个犯人各抽<span lang="EN-US">30</span>鞭子等残暴迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日在绵阳市再次被抓捕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，在四川女子监狱遭吊在钢管上毒打，被强制戴手铐脚镣、关小号、不准睡觉等酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日上午，绵阳市法轮功学员柳涛与三台县法轮功学员邓成开到三台县芦溪镇去买东西被抓捕。柳涛被关押在绵阳市看守所，邓成开被关押在三台县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，柳涛、邓承开被绵阳市三台县法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚金二千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">龙克海：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，又名龙刻海，甘肃省徽县嘉陵镇嘉陵村人，基督徒，陕西省宝鸡市长驻居民，民主维权公民，中国曾押政治犯。因为人急公好义，忧国忧民，且信仰基督教，经常参加成都秋雨之福教会的聚会活动，随广受他人赞誉；积极参与各种公民圈活动而曾数次遭到警方“喝茶”、警告；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾因民主聚会而被甘肃省徽县警方以“寻衅滋事罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；获释后，因不断向当地法院提出抗诉并要求警方予以国家赔偿，遭到当局的进一步憎恨和报复；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被陕西省宝鸡市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”抓捕，后转正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案件被地方检察院起诉至陕西省宝鸡市渭滨区法院，指控其在<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Facebook</span>发布和转发一系列诽谤侮辱中共领导人及辱骂中国共产党的言论信息，严重破坏社会秩序，因而构成寻衅滋事罪；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其案在陕西省宝鸡市渭滨区法院不公开审理；<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，在不允许家属旁听的情况下，被该法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，提起上诉，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，经陕西省宝鸡市中级法院二审裁决，依然维持原判；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，刑满释放。此前羁押于宝鸡市渭滨区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初，甘肃陇南徽县民主维权人士龙克海被甘肃国保从宝鸡带走后，一直没有讯息。后获悉，龙克海已被刑拘。有朋友打通甘肃国宝电话得知，确定龙已被刑拘。国保不愿透露罪名，只说刑拘通知书已给龙的亲属。朋友估计罪名是寻衅滋事罪，可能与龙克海前阵前往陕西凤县围观常玮平开庭有关。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日甘徽县法院以犯寻衅滋事罪判龙克海有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年， 刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。目前龙克海被羁押在甘肃徽县看守所<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_71.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_71.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/2.html"><b align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖南省长沙市开福区法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1952</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月刚出家门，被一伙警察抓捕至长沙市第四看守所关押。于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月开庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/14/449565.html</span></u><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">娄亚红：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">许昌市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>年生。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，娄亚红曾被关进洗脑班迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，娄亚红被警察从家中抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，被许昌市魏都区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，勒索<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元。娄亚红上诉后，被中级法院维持原判。如今，娄亚红已被投入新乡女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E5%AE%B6%E6%9C%89%E2%80%9C%E5%A4%A9%E8%B5%90%E6%B4%AA%E7%A6%8F%E2%80%9D%E5%AF%B9%E8%81%94-%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%A8%84%E4%BA%9A%E7%BA%A2%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434020.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E5%AE%B6%E6%9C%89%E2%80%9C%E5%A4%A9%E8%B5%90%E6%B4%AA%E7%A6%8F%E2%80%9D%E5%AF%B9%E8%81%94-%E6%B2%B3%E5%8D%97%E5%A8%84%E4%BA%9A%E7%BA%A2%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434020.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢桂芬：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北涞水县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1940</span>年代生人，家住涞水县王村乡辛庄头村的农家妇女。在中共对法轮功持续至今与二十一年的迫害中，屡遭中共迫害，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日再次被警察抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。目前卢桂芬老人仍被非法关押在保定看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">卢巧丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-style: italic; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，广东揭阳法轮功学员。揭阳市揭东区桂岭镇人，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，被榕城区国保和东升派出所警察抓捕，关押于揭阳市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年底，她被揭东区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，她被关押到广东省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/7/2022-3-7.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">卢永良：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南岳阳市法轮功学员，男，<span lang="EN-US">1958</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日下午，卢永良在家中与几位法轮功学员一起读法轮大法著作。被警察入户抓捕，并抄家。电脑、打印机、刻录机、大法书籍、真相资料等私人物品被警察抄走。后遭刑事拘留、批捕、起诉。卢永良被关押一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被湖南省平江县法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，并勒索罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元，没收电脑、打印机、刻录机、装订机等。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卢志英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午案受害人。<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">2020</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：卢志英被判</span>有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">30</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">陆大新：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">长春法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1967</span>年生，又名陆大欣、陆方兰。早年修炼法轮大法后，按真、善、忍标准做好人，身心受益。一九九九年，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，她曾三次被抓捕、两次被劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，陆大新（陆方兰）被吉林警察抓捕，一直被关押在看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，陆大新被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，已经转至吉林女子监狱迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/8/452868.html</span></u></b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">陆辉煌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，壮族，<span lang="EN-US">1978</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，户籍所在地：广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡上瑶村方和屯<span lang="EN-US">94</span>号。曾在广东珠三角等地工作，工作之余关心国家、民生状况，进行写作并在网络上传播。<span lang="EN-US">2013 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 10 </span>月，其写了《致中共中央公开信——关于政治体制改革的思考和建议》，在文中分析了国家的政治体制并建议中共中央进行宪政改革<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 3 </span>月，其写了《“妄议”国事》一文，在文中批评了个别国家领导人和政策。<span lang="EN-US">2016 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 6 </span>月，其写下《致习近平总书记的公开信》，呼吁习近平关注、关心农民工。以上三篇文章只是在一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群和一些<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>好友中传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 1 </span>月，其写了《对当前政局的分析与呼吁》，在文中分析了当时的时局，反对修宪和个人崇拜，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信、邮箱传播，并向《北京之春》网站投稿，《北京之春》网站分别于<span lang="EN-US"> 2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">25 </span>日和<span lang="EN-US"> 2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 28 </span>日分上篇和下篇刊登了该文。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7 </span>月，其写作《“艰时克共”的建议》，呼吁早日促进《零八宪章》的目标实现，并通过微信群传播，后又在《北京之春》网站刊登。<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US"> 7</span>月，其写了《致“中国劳工观察”组织的信》，在文中描述了中国劳工特别是农民工的真实情况，并请求“中国劳工观察”组织帮助他们维权，并通过<span lang="EN-US"> QQ </span>、微信，向朋友传播。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其在深圳富士康鸿观厂区被深圳市龙华区公安分局福民派出所传唤到该派出所。（<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在签刑事拘留通知书时，其知道并没有人报案，他们是根据上级部门监控发现深圳有人传播所谓政治不当言论的线索，并依据文章的线索传唤。）在派出所里，警察在还没立案（也就是说还没进入刑事阶段）之前，就利用威胁（不说就打）手段获取其手机、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱等密码，并利用这些密码非法登录其<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱，搜集其所谓犯罪证据。就这样，公安机关在其手机便签、<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>、微信、邮箱搜集到了前面其所列举的六篇文章。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，公安机关以这六篇文章作为证据开始立案，将其刑事拘留，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日将其逮捕，之后经过两次退回补充侦查，三次延长审查起诉。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，深圳市龙华检察院以所谓的散布虚假信息、辱骂国家领导人、造谣污蔑国家的政治体制、法律制度、基本国策、指导思想、战略布局、反腐斗争、发展路线、劳工制度与现状、民族复兴目标等，涉嫌寻衅滋事罪起诉，所谓的罪证就是其前面列举的六篇文章。由于其坚持不认罪，并在里面坚持斗争，遭遇了杨伟东恶警施加的电击、禁食、戴镣铐等酷刑。并且不准其与家人通信。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日（接到起诉书的第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天），在深圳市龙华法院开庭前会议，就证据的合法性进行质疑。由于家人没有给其请律师，其律师是官派的，在这次庭前会议上根本没有就证据的合法性为其辩护。而陆辉煌本人就检方的证据提出三个疑点：<span lang="EN-US">1</span>、其写的文章属于言论自由的范畴。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>、检方的证据是利用非法手段（威胁手段）取得的。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>、检方指控其在《北京之春》刊发文章，也是通过翻墙的手段获得的，根据《宪法》人人平等的原则，公检法等机关并没有特权，他们能用的，咱们平民百姓也能用。他们能翻墙，咱平民百姓也能翻墙，那就没有必要浪费大量纳税人的钱去建所谓的“防火墙”了。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，在深圳市龙华法院正式开庭。其本人写的辩护词不让其带到法庭。在上车去法庭时，法警给其戴上头套，只露出眼睛，到了法院才摘下来。在庭审时，审判长江涛以不准辱骂国家领导人为由阻止其为自己辩护。庭审只用了大约一个小时就草草结束。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其接到判决书，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年半，由于在看守所长期睡地板，导致其得了风湿，腰椎疾病。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被调往广东省从化监狱服刑，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日刑满释放。释放后多次申诉无果。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点，广西异议人士陆辉煌在南宁市大岭新村居住地被多名不明身份男子带走。<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日上午，朋友拨打不通陆辉煌电话，致电陆辉煌户籍所在地广西贵港市桂平市垌心乡派出所询问，接线员否认有抓陆辉煌，但言语闪烁其词。陆辉煌曾因言论获刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月刑满释放。有网友猜测陆辉煌被再次带走，或与其签名呼吁彻查徐州铁链女奴事件有关。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，陆辉煌被广西壮族自治区贵港市法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日；其不服，已表示上诉。目前被羁押于广西贵港市看守所（广西壮族自治区贵港市港南区八塘镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">537131</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/46.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_19.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/02/blog-post_19.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">陆建华：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1960</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，上海市人，前中国最高层核心智囊之一，第二届“北京市十大杰出青年”，曾任中国社会科学院社会学研究所研究员、公共政策研究中心副主任，中央电视台特约评论员和重庆市渝北区副区长等职，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年起，因陆续为香港记者程翔提供<span lang="EN-US">70</span>余篇稿件，其中<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月所提供的<span lang="EN-US">4</span>篇文章内容被中共视为涉及“国家绝密资料”，遂于<span lang="EN-US"> 2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被国家安全局秘密拘捕；后经秘密审判，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被北京市第二中级法院以“泄露国家机密罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 20</span>年；其上诉坚称自己被冤，均被驳回。目前在北京市监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陆建荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏讨薪农民工、维权公民。曾在<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年、<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年先后两次于六四敏感日因转发中国公民及国际友人在驻美中国大使馆门口举行纪念“六<span lang="EN-US">.</span>四”活动的图片遭到警方传唤。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日又被江苏警方跨省抓捕，涉嫌“非法买卖枪支弹药罪”，至今不被释放，被刑拘于泰兴市看守所。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">路朝波：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江大庆市林甸县法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。林甸县实验小学教师。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2020</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，由黑龙江省公安厅“督办”，大庆市公安局和林甸县公安局出动五十多个便衣警察，暴力抓捕了大庆市林甸县法轮功学员薛丽威、王玉红、路朝波、董娜、陈卫波等。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，大庆让胡路区法院枉法判决：路朝波、王玉红被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。薛丽威、陈卫波被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年、罚款四万元，董娜被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月、罚款三万元。关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。路朝波刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/30/454021.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family:
